      SUM(CASE WHEN n >= 10 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)                        AS power_users
    FROM seen
  `).bind(target, d1, d7, d14, d30, d7, d14, d14, d30, d30).first();

  // Lapsed-then-returned in the last 7d: a session in the last 7d, a session older
  // than 30d, and nothing in the 30d->7d gap.
  const reactivated = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS n FROM sessions s
    WHERE target = ? AND joined_at >= ?
      AND user_id IN (SELECT user_id FROM sessions WHERE target = ? AND joined_at < ?)
      AND user_id NOT IN (SELECT user_id FROM sessions WHERE target = ? AND joined_at >= ? AND joined_at < ?)
  `).bind(target, d7, target, d30, target, d30, d7).first();

  const buckets = await env.DB.prepare(`
    WITH seen AS (SELECT user_id, COUNT(*) AS n FROM sessions WHERE target = ? GROUP BY user_id)
    SELECT
      CASE WHEN n = 1 THEN '1' WHEN n <= 4 THEN '2-4' WHEN n <= 9 THEN '5-9'
           WHEN n <= 24 THEN '10-24' ELSE '25+' END AS bucket,
      COUNT(*) AS count
    FROM seen GROUP BY bucket
  `).bind(target).all();

  return json({
    target, days,
    acquisition: acquisition.results || [],
    churn: {
      active1: (churn && churn.active1) || 0,
      active7: (churn && churn.active7) || 0,
      active14: (churn && churn.active14) || 0,
      active30: (churn && churn.active30) || 0,
      lapsed_7_14: (churn && churn.lapsed_7_14) || 0,
      lapsed_14_30: (churn && churn.lapsed_14_30) || 0,
      lapsed_30p: (churn && churn.lapsed_30p) || 0,
      reactivated7: (reactivated && reactivated.n) || 0,
    },
    lifetime: {
      total: (churn && churn.total_players) || 0,
      avgDays: Math.round(((churn && churn.avg_lifetime_days) || 0) * 10) / 10,
      avgSessions: Math.round(((churn && churn.avg_sessions) || 0) * 10) / 10,
      powerUsers: (churn && churn.power_users) || 0,
    },
    sessionBuckets: buckets.results || [],
  });
}

// ============================================================================
// /stats/heatmap — sessions by UTC weekday x hour, to find the best play times.
// ============================================================================
async function handleStatsHeatmap(_request, env, url) {
  const days = parseDays(url, 30);
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));
  const cutoff = nowUnix() - days * 86400;

  const result = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT
      CAST(strftime('%w', joined_at, 'unixepoch', '${TZ_SQL}') AS INTEGER) AS dow,
      CAST(strftime('%H', joined_at, 'unixepoch', '${TZ_SQL}') AS INTEGER) AS hour,
      COUNT(*) AS count
    FROM sessions
    WHERE target = ? AND joined_at >= ?
    GROUP BY dow, hour
  `).bind(target, cutoff).all();

  return json({ target, days, cells: result.results || [] });
}

// ============================================================================
// /stats/session-split — new vs returning session length over time, plus a
// session-length histogram.
// ============================================================================
async function handleStatsSessionSplit(_request, env, url) {
  const days = parseDays(url, 30);
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));
  const cutoff = nowUnix() - days * 86400;

  const daily = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT
      strftime('%Y-%m-%d', joined_at, 'unixepoch', '${TZ_SQL}') AS date,
      AVG(CASE WHEN is_new = 1 THEN duration_s END) / 60.0 AS new_avg,
      AVG(CASE WHEN is_new = 0 THEN duration_s END) / 60.0 AS ret_avg
    FROM sessions
    WHERE target = ? AND joined_at >= ? AND duration_s IS NOT NULL
    GROUP BY date
    ORDER BY date ASC
  `).bind(target, cutoff).all();

  const hist = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT
      CASE WHEN duration_s < 60 THEN '<1m' WHEN duration_s < 300 THEN '1-5m'
           WHEN duration_s < 600 THEN '5-10m' WHEN duration_s < 1800 THEN '10-30m'
           WHEN duration_s < 3600 THEN '30-60m' ELSE '60m+' END AS bucket,
      COUNT(*) AS count
    FROM sessions
    WHERE target = ? AND joined_at >= ? AND duration_s IS NOT NULL
    GROUP BY bucket
  `).bind(target, cutoff).all();

  return json({ target, days, rows: daily.results || [], histogram: hist.results || [] });
}

// ============================================================================
// /stats/milestones — onboarding/progression funnel: distinct players who ever
// reached each milestone, against the new-player baseline.
// ============================================================================
async function handleStatsMilestones(_request, env, url) {
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));

  const rows = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT milestone, COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS users
    FROM milestones WHERE target = ?
    GROUP BY milestone ORDER BY users DESC
  `).bind(target).all();

  const base = await env.DB.prepare(
    "SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS joined FROM sessions WHERE target = ? AND is_new = 1",
  ).bind(target).first();

  return json({ target, joined: (base && base.joined) || 0, rows: rows.results || [] });
}

// ============================================================================
// /stats/servers — health of servers reporting fresh heartbeats right now.
// ============================================================================
// ============================================================================
// /admin/servers — live servers (with player names) for the command-targeting
// dropdown. Admin-token protected. Like /stats/servers but includes names.
// ============================================================================
async function handleAdminServersList(_request, env, url) {
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));
  const freshAfter = nowUnix() - HEARTBEAT_FRESHNESS_SECONDS;
  const result = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT server_id, player_count, players_json, last_heartbeat
    FROM live_servers
    WHERE target = ? AND last_heartbeat >= ?
    ORDER BY player_count DESC
  `).bind(target, freshAfter).all();
  const servers = (result.results || []).map((r) => {
    let players = [];
    try {
      const arr = JSON.parse(r.players_json || "[]");
      players = arr.map((pp) => (pp && (pp.username || pp.name)) || null).filter(Boolean);
    } catch (e) {}
    return { serverId: r.server_id, players, count: r.player_count || players.length };
  });
  return json({ target, servers });
}

async function handleStatsServers(_request, env, url) {
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));
  const freshAfter = nowUnix() - HEARTBEAT_FRESHNESS_SECONDS;

  const result = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT server_id, player_count, uptime_seconds, last_heartbeat
    FROM live_servers
    WHERE target = ? AND last_heartbeat >= ?
    ORDER BY player_count DESC
  `).bind(target, freshAfter).all();

  const servers = (result.results || []).map((r) => ({
    serverId: r.server_id,
    players: r.player_count || 0,
    uptimeSeconds: r.uptime_seconds || 0,
  }));
  const totalPlayers = servers.reduce((a, s) => a + s.players, 0);

  return json({
    target,
    serverCount: servers.length,
    totalPlayers,
    avgPlayers: servers.length ? Math.round((totalPlayers / servers.length) * 10) / 10 : 0,
    servers,
  });
}

// ============================================================================
// /stats/coinflow — cumulative coin balance (faucet minus sink) plus who is
// spending: spender rate, average spend per spender, and the top spenders.
// ============================================================================
async function handleStatsCoinflow(_request, env, url) {
  const days = parseDays(url, 30);
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));
  const cutoff = nowUnix() - days * 86400;

  const daily = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT
      strftime('%Y-%m-%d', created_at, 'unixepoch', '${TZ_SQL}') AS date,
      SUM(CASE WHEN direction = 'earn' THEN amount ELSE 0 END)  AS earned,
      SUM(CASE WHEN direction = 'spend' THEN amount ELSE 0 END) AS spent
    FROM coin_events
    WHERE target = ? AND created_at >= ?
    GROUP BY date ORDER BY date ASC
  `).bind(target, cutoff).all();

  const totals = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT
      COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN direction = 'spend' THEN user_id END) AS spenders,
      COUNT(DISTINCT user_id)                                        AS participants,
      SUM(CASE WHEN direction = 'spend' THEN amount ELSE 0 END)      AS total_spent
    FROM coin_events
    WHERE target = ? AND created_at >= ?
  `).bind(target, cutoff).first();

  const whales = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT user_id, username, SUM(amount) AS spent
    FROM coin_events
    WHERE target = ? AND created_at >= ? AND direction = 'spend'
    GROUP BY user_id ORDER BY spent DESC LIMIT 15
  `).bind(target, cutoff).all();

  const spenders = (totals && totals.spenders) || 0;
  const participants = (totals && totals.participants) || 0;
  const totalSpent = (totals && totals.total_spent) || 0;

  return json({
    target, days,
    rows: daily.results || [],
    spenders, participants,
    spenderRate: participants > 0 ? Math.round((spenders / participants) * 1000) / 10 : 0,
    avgSpendPerSpender: spenders > 0 ? Math.round(totalSpent / spenders) : 0,
    whales: whales.results || [],
  });
}

// ============================================================================
// /stats/shop-detail — revenue split by currency and item kind, repeat-purchase
// rate, and average time from first join to first purchase.
// ============================================================================
async function handleStatsShopDetail(_request, env, url) {
  const days = parseDays(url, 30);
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));
  const cutoff = nowUnix() - days * 86400;

  const byCurrency = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT COALESCE(currency, 'unknown') AS currency, COUNT(*) AS purchases, SUM(price) AS revenue
    FROM shop_events
    WHERE target = ? AND created_at >= ? AND event = 'purchase'
    GROUP BY currency ORDER BY purchases DESC
  `).bind(target, cutoff).all();

  const byKind = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT COALESCE(item_kind, 'unknown') AS kind, COUNT(*) AS purchases, SUM(price) AS revenue
    FROM shop_events
    WHERE target = ? AND created_at >= ? AND event = 'purchase'
    GROUP BY kind ORDER BY purchases DESC
  `).bind(target, cutoff).all();

  const repeat = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT COUNT(*) AS buyers, SUM(CASE WHEN c > 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS repeat_buyers
    FROM (
      SELECT user_id, COUNT(*) AS c FROM shop_events
      WHERE target = ? AND created_at >= ? AND event = 'purchase'
      GROUP BY user_id
    )
  `).bind(target, cutoff).first();

  const ttf = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT AVG((fp.first_purchase - s.first_join) / 86400.0) AS avg_days
    FROM (SELECT user_id, MIN(created_at) AS first_purchase FROM shop_events
          WHERE target = ? AND event = 'purchase' GROUP BY user_id) fp
    JOIN (SELECT user_id, MIN(joined_at) AS first_join FROM sessions
          WHERE target = ? GROUP BY user_id) s ON s.user_id = fp.user_id
    WHERE fp.first_purchase >= s.first_join
  `).bind(target, target).first();

  const buyers = (repeat && repeat.buyers) || 0;
  const repeatBuyers = (repeat && repeat.repeat_buyers) || 0;

  return json({
    target, days,
    byCurrency: byCurrency.results || [],
    byKind: byKind.results || [],
    buyers, repeatBuyers,
    repeatRate: buyers > 0 ? Math.round((repeatBuyers / buyers) * 1000) / 10 : 0,
    avgDaysToFirstPurchase: Math.round(((ttf && ttf.avg_days) || 0) * 10) / 10,
  });
}

// ============================================================================
// /stats/streaks — distribution of each player's best daily-claim streak, plus
// which reward sets actually drop.
// ============================================================================
async function handleStatsStreaks(_request, env, url) {
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));

  const buckets = await env.DB.prepare(`
    WITH mx AS (SELECT user_id, MAX(streak) AS s FROM daily_claims WHERE target = ? GROUP BY user_id)
    SELECT
      CASE WHEN s <= 1 THEN '1' WHEN s <= 3 THEN '2-3' WHEN s <= 6 THEN '4-6'
           WHEN s <= 13 THEN '7-13' WHEN s <= 29 THEN '14-29' ELSE '30+' END AS bucket,
      COUNT(*) AS count
    FROM mx GROUP BY bucket
  `).bind(target).all();

  const sets = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT COALESCE(set_name, 'unknown') AS set_name, COUNT(*) AS drops, COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS players
    FROM daily_claims
    WHERE target = ? AND reward_type = 'block_set'
    GROUP BY set_name ORDER BY drops DESC
  `).bind(target).all();

  return json({ target, buckets: buckets.results || [], sets: sets.results || [] });
}

// ============================================================================
// /stats/plus-quality — how many Plus taps are "wasted" on already-subscribed
// players, split by where the tap came from.
// ============================================================================
async function handleStatsPlusQuality(_request, env, url) {
  const days = parseDays(url, 30);
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));
  const cutoff = nowUnix() - days * 86400;

  const totals = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT
      SUM(CASE WHEN event = 'tap' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)                      AS taps,
      SUM(CASE WHEN event = 'tap' AND already_plus = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS wasted,
      SUM(CASE WHEN event = 'tap' AND already_plus = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS prospects,
      SUM(CASE WHEN event = 'purchase' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)                AS purchases
    FROM plus_events WHERE target = ? AND created_at >= ?
  `).bind(target, cutoff).first();

  const sources = await env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT
      COALESCE(source, 'unknown') AS source,
      SUM(CASE WHEN event = 'tap' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)                      AS taps,
      SUM(CASE WHEN event = 'tap' AND already_plus = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS wasted,
      SUM(CASE WHEN event = 'purchase' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)                AS purchases
    FROM plus_events WHERE target = ? AND created_at >= ?
    GROUP BY source ORDER BY taps DESC
  `).bind(target, cutoff).all();

  const taps = (totals && totals.taps) || 0;
  const wasted = (totals && totals.wasted) || 0;

  return json({
    target, days,
    taps,
    wasted,
    prospects: (totals && totals.prospects) || 0,
    purchases: (totals && totals.purchases) || 0,
    wastedRate: taps > 0 ? Math.round((wasted / taps) * 1000) / 10 : 0,
    sources: sources.results || [],
  });
}

// ============================================================================
// /stats/block-trends — block popularity over time, pivoted to the top movers.
// Reads block_history (filled best-effort on each top-blocks ingest). Wrapped so
// it returns empty until the table is created.
// ============================================================================
async function handleStatsBlockTrends(_request, env, url) {
  const days = parseDays(url, 30);
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));
  const cutoffDate = localDateStr(nowUnix() - days * 86400);
  try {
    const res = await env.DB.prepare(
      "SELECT date, block_name, count FROM block_history WHERE target = ? AND date >= ? ORDER BY date ASC",
    ).bind(target, cutoffDate).all();
    const rows = res.results || [];
    const dates = [];
    const seen = {};
    const byBlock = {};
    for (const r of rows) {
      if (!seen[r.date]) { seen[r.date] = 1; dates.push(r.date); }
      if (!byBlock[r.block_name]) byBlock[r.block_name] = {};
      byBlock[r.block_name][r.date] = r.count;
    }
    const blocks = Object.keys(byBlock).map((name) => {
      const counts = dates.map((d) => (byBlock[name][d] != null ? byBlock[name][d] : 0));
      const present = counts.filter((c) => c > 0);
      const first = present.length ? present[0] : 0;
      const last = counts.length ? counts[counts.length - 1] : 0;
      const peak = counts.length ? Math.max.apply(null, counts) : 0;
      return { name: name, counts: counts, peak: peak, last: last, delta: last - first };
    }).sort((a, b) => b.peak - a.peak).slice(0, 6);
    return json({ target: target, days: days, dates: dates, blocks: blocks });
  } catch (err) {
    return json({ target: target, days: days, dates: [], blocks: [] });
  }
}

// ============================================================================
// /stats/engagement-trends — daily average coins/likes/playtime/streak across
// online players, sampled from heartbeats into engagement_history.
// ============================================================================
async function handleStatsEngagementTrends(_request, env, url) {
  const days = parseDays(url, 30);
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));
  const cutoffDate = localDateStr(nowUnix() - days * 86400);
  try {
    const res = await env.DB.prepare(
      "SELECT date, players, avg_coins, avg_likes, avg_playtime, avg_streak, max_coins, max_streak FROM engagement_history WHERE target = ? AND date >= ? ORDER BY date ASC",
    ).bind(target, cutoffDate).all();
    return json({ target: target, days: days, rows: res.results || [] });
  } catch (err) {
    return json({ target: target, days: days, rows: [] });
  }
}

// ============================================================================
// /stats/slots-trends — saves-per-player distribution snapshotted daily into
// slots_history on each slot-count ingest.
// ============================================================================
async function handleStatsSlotsTrends(_request, env, url) {
  const days = parseDays(url, 30);
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));
  const cutoffDate = localDateStr(nowUnix() - days * 86400);
  try {
    const res = await env.DB.prepare(
      "SELECT date, total_players, avg_slots, multi_slot_rate FROM slots_history WHERE target = ? AND date >= ? ORDER BY date ASC",
    ).bind(target, cutoffDate).all();
    return json({ target: target, days: days, rows: res.results || [] });
  } catch (err) {
    return json({ target: target, days: days, rows: [] });
  }
}

// ============================================================================
// Chat capture. The game batch-POSTs in-game chat to /chat; we keyword-tag each
// line immediately (so there's always a category), then Workers AI refines it on
// demand via /chat/classify. Old rows auto-purge after 30 days.
// ============================================================================
const CHAT_RETENTION_DAYS = 30;

// Fast, deterministic first-pass tagger. AI (ai_category) overrides this in the
// dashboard once classified. is_complaint is what the "complaints" view keys on.
function keywordClassifyChat(text) {
  const t = " " + String(text || "").toLowerCase() + " ";
  const has = (arr) => arr.some((w) => t.indexOf(w) !== -1);
  const bug = ["bug", "glitch", "broke", "broken", "not working", "doesnt work", "doesn't work", "dont work", "won't load", "wont load", "cant load", "error", " lag", "laggy", "frozen", "freeze", "crash", "stuck", "disappear", "deleted", "lost my", "reset my", "wiped", "gone"];
  const complaint = ["hate", "worst", "terrible", "annoying", "unfair", "boring", " bad ", "trash", "sucks", "scam", "rip off", "ripoff", "too expensive", "pay to win", "p2w", "fix this", "please fix", "why cant", "why can't", "ripped off"];
  const toxic = ["noob", "loser", "idiot", "shut up", "stfu", "kys", "stupid", "dumb"];
  const suggestion = ["should add", "you should", "can you add", "please add", "add a ", "add more", "wish there was", "would be cool", "suggest", "maybe add", "pls add", "plz add"];
  const praise = ["love", "awesome", "amazing", "great", "best", " cool", "epic", " fun", "nice", "thank", "tysm", "goated", " fire", "w game", "peak", "the goat"];
  if (has(toxic)) return { category: "toxic", isComplaint: 1 };
  if (has(bug)) return { category: "bug", isComplaint: 1 };
  if (has(complaint)) return { category: "complaint", isComplaint: 1 };
  if (has(suggestion)) return { category: "suggestion", isComplaint: 0 };
  if (String(text || "").trim().endsWith("?") || has(["how do i", "how to", "where is", "what is", "is there", "how much"])) return { category: "question", isComplaint: 0 };
  if (has(praise)) return { category: "praise", isComplaint: 0 };
  return { category: "chatter", isComplaint: 0 };
}

async function handleChatIngest(request, env) {
  const ingest = request.headers.get("X-Ingest-Token");
  if (!ingest || ingest !== env.INGEST_TOKEN) {
    return json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, 401);
  }

  let body;
  try {
    body = await request.json();
  } catch {
    return json({ error: "Invalid JSON" }, 400);
  }

  const targetKey = parseTarget(body.target);
  const messages = Array.isArray(body.messages) ? body.messages.slice(0, 100) : null;
  if (!messages) return json({ error: "Missing messages[]" }, 400);

  const stmts = [];
  for (const m of messages) {
    const text = String(m.text || "").slice(0, 280);
    if (!text) continue;
    const tag = keywordClassifyChat(text);
    const ts = Number.parseInt(m.ts, 10) || nowUnix();
    const msgId = m.msgId ? String(m.msgId).slice(0, 48) : (String(m.userId || "0") + "-" + ts + "-" + text.length);
    stmts.push(env.DB.prepare(`
      INSERT OR IGNORE INTO chat_messages
        (target, msg_id, user_id, username, message, category, is_complaint, created_at)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
    `).bind(
      targetKey, msgId, m.userId || null,
      String(m.username || "").slice(0, 64), text, tag.category, tag.isComplaint, ts,
    ));
  }

  try {
    if (stmts.length > 0) await env.DB.batch(stmts);
  } catch (err) {
    // chat_messages not migrated yet — don't fail the game's POST.
    return json({ ok: true, stored: 0, warning: "chat_messages unavailable" });
  }

  // Best-effort retention sweep, occasionally.
  if (Math.random() < 0.05) {
    try {
      await env.DB.prepare("DELETE FROM chat_messages WHERE created_at < ?")
        .bind(nowUnix() - CHAT_RETENTION_DAYS * 86400).run();
    } catch (err) { /* table absent */ }
  }

  return json({ ok: true, stored: stmts.length });
}

// Workers AI refinement. Pulls a batch of still-unclassified lines, classifies
// them in ONE model call (cheap), writes ai_category + sentiment back. Returns
// gracefully if the [ai] binding isn't configured yet.
async function handleChatClassify(_request, env, url) {
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));
  if (!env.AI) {
    return json({ error: "Workers AI binding not configured", classified: 0, remaining: 0 });
  }

  let pending;
  try {
    pending = await env.DB.prepare(
      "SELECT id, message FROM chat_messages WHERE target = ? AND ai_category IS NULL ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 20",
    ).bind(target).all();
  } catch (err) {
    return json({ error: "chat_messages unavailable", classified: 0, remaining: 0 });
  }
  const rows = pending.results || [];
  if (!rows.length) return json({ classified: 0, remaining: 0 });

  const list = rows.map((r, i) => (i + 1) + ". " + String(r.message).replace(/\s+/g, " ").slice(0, 200)).join("\n");
  const sys = "You classify short Roblox game chat messages. For each numbered message return a category from exactly this set: complaint, bug, praise, suggestion, question, social, toxic, other — and a sentiment from: positive, negative, neutral. 'complaint' = unhappy/criticism, 'bug' = something broken, 'toxic' = insults/harassment, 'social' = small talk. Respond ONLY with a JSON array like [{\"i\":1,\"category\":\"bug\",\"sentiment\":\"negative\"}]. No prose.";

  const out = await aiComplete(env, sys, list, 1024);
  if (out == null) {
    return json({ error: "AI call failed or not configured", classified: 0, remaining: rows.length });
  }

  let parsed = [];
  try {
    const m = String(out).match(/\[[\s\S]*\]/);
    parsed = m ? JSON.parse(m[0]) : [];
  } catch (err) {
    return json({ error: "Could not parse AI output", classified: 0, remaining: rows.length });
  }

  const COMPLAINT = { complaint: 1, bug: 1, toxic: 1 };
  const VALID = { complaint: 1, bug: 1, praise: 1, suggestion: 1, question: 1, social: 1, toxic: 1, other: 1 };
  const updates = [];
  for (const p of parsed) {
    const idx = Number.parseInt(p.i, 10) - 1;
    if (idx < 0 || idx >= rows.length) continue;
    const cat = VALID[p.category] ? p.category : "other";
    const sent = ["positive", "negative", "neutral"].indexOf(p.sentiment) !== -1 ? p.sentiment : "neutral";
    updates.push(env.DB.prepare(
      "UPDATE chat_messages SET ai_category = ?, sentiment = ?, is_complaint = ? WHERE id = ?",
    ).bind(cat, sent, COMPLAINT[cat] ? 1 : 0, rows[idx].id));
  }
  try {
    if (updates.length > 0) await env.DB.batch(updates);
  } catch (err) {
    return json({ error: "write-back failed", classified: 0, remaining: rows.length });
  }

  const left = await env.DB.prepare(
    "SELECT COUNT(*) AS n FROM chat_messages WHERE target = ? AND ai_category IS NULL",
  ).bind(target).first();
  return json({ classified: updates.length, remaining: (left && left.n) || 0 });
}

// Read: volume over time, category breakdown, totals, and a filterable feed.
async function handleStatsChat(_request, env, url) {
  const days = parseDays(url, 30);
  const target = parseTarget(url.searchParams.get("target"));
  const cutoff = nowUnix() - days * 86400;
  const category = url.searchParams.get("category") || "";
  const complaintsOnly = url.searchParams.get("complaints") === "1";
  const q = (url.searchParams.get("q") || "").slice(0, 60);

  try {
    const daily = await env.DB.prepare(`
      SELECT strftime('%Y-%m-%d', created_at, 'unixepoch', '${TZ_SQL}') AS date,
             COUNT(*) AS total,
             SUM(is_complaint) AS complaints
      FROM chat_messages
      WHERE target = ? AND created_at >= ?
      GROUP BY date ORDER BY date ASC
    `).bind(target, cutoff).all();

    const cats = await env.DB.prepare(`
      SELECT COALESCE(ai_category, category) AS category, COUNT(*) AS count
      FROM chat_messages
      WHERE target = ? AND created_at >= ?
      GROUP BY category ORDER BY count DESC
    `).bind(target, cutoff).all();

    const totals = await env.DB.prepare(`
      SELECT COUNT(*) AS total,
             SUM(is_complaint) AS complaints,
             SUM(CASE WHEN ai_category IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS unclassified
      FROM chat_messages WHERE target = ? AND created_at >= ?
    `).bind(target, cutoff).first();

    // Feed with optional filters, built with bound params only.
    const cond = ["target = ?", "created_at >= ?"];
    const binds = [target, cutoff];
    if (complaintsOnly) cond.push("is_complaint = 1");
    if (category) { cond.push("COALESCE(ai_category, category) = ?"); binds.push(category); }
    if (q) { cond.push("message LIKE ?"); binds.push("%" + q + "%"); }
    const feed = await env.DB.prepare(
      "SELECT user_id, username, message, COALESCE(ai_category, category) AS category, sentiment, is_complaint, created_at"
      + " FROM chat_messages WHERE " + cond.join(" AND ")
      + " ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 120",
    ).bind(...binds).all();

    return json({
      target, days,
      rows: daily.results || [],
      categories: cats.results || [],
      totals: {
        total: (totals && totals.total) || 0,
        complaints: (totals && totals.complaints) || 0,
        unclassified: (totals && totals.unclassified) || 0,
      },
      feed: feed.results || [],
    });
  } catch (err) {
    return json({ target, days, rows: [], categories: [], totals: { total: 0, complaints: 0, unclassified: 0 }, feed: [] });
  }
}

// ============================================================================
// In-game help bot. The game forwards question-like chat to /chat/help; Workers
// AI answers ONLY from the How to Play guide (HELP_GUIDE). It returns one of:
//   answer -> a short reply to show privately in the asker's chat
//   guide  -> a nudge to open the How to Play book (the game also flashes it)
//   none   -> not a covered how-to question; the game stays silent
// Keep HELP_GUIDE in sync with HelpBookUI if the in-game guide changes.
// ============================================================================
const HELP_GUIDE = [
  "MOVEMENT - Walk: move around your plot (PC: WASD, Mobile: joystick). Jump: hop onto blocks (PC: Space, Mobile: jump button). Sprint: hold to run faster (PC: hold Ctrl, Mobile: sprint button). Fly: jump twice to start flying and jump twice again to land (Mobile: tap the fly button, with up/down arrows).",
  "PLACE A BLOCK: point and click - or tap on mobile - where you want it and it snaps into place (PC: right click, Mobile: tap).",
  "BREAK A BLOCK: hold on the block to break it, and keep holding to break more (PC: hold left click, Mobile: tap and hold).",
  "MOBILE SLABS AND DOORS: tap once to show a ghost block, tap the ghost to place it, tap X to cancel; tap the lock button to save how the ghost sits so one tap places it that way.",
  "INVENTORY AND HOTBAR: open your inventory to see all your blocks (PC: E, Mobile: inventory button). Click or tap a block to add it to your hotbar. Remove a block from the hotbar with right click or Q. Quick-move items into chests and crafting tables with Shift+click. On mobile, double-tap an item to delete it, and hold then drag to move items.",
  "SHOVEL: use it on grass to make a path block (PC: right click grass, Mobile: tap grass).",
  "SHEARS: snip leaves into bare branches, snip vines to stop them growing, and snip sugar cane to stop it (PC: right click, Mobile: tap).",
  "SLABS: aim at the top or bottom of a block for a flat slab, or aim at a side for a standing slab.",
  "DOORS: place or open a door by right clicking it (tap on mobile). Doors snap to 6 spots on a block and always line up with your wall.",
  "FENCES: they hook onto nearby blocks automatically; right click a fence (tap on mobile) to unhook it, and again to re-hook.",
  "FRAME BLOCKS: place a frame (it starts empty), then use it on any solid block (PC: right click, Mobile: tap) to copy that block\'s look. Wallpaper frames are flat for floors, walls and ceilings, and you can still build on them.",
  "TREES AND GROWING: most saplings only need 1 to grow, but big trees - Redwood and Dark Oak - need 4 saplings planted in a 2x2 square. Trees need open space above them to grow.",
].join("\n");

const HELP_PROMPT_PREFIX =
  "You are a friendly in-game help bot for a Roblox block-building game, talking to young players. "
  + "Use ONLY the GUIDE below; never invent features. Reply with ONE JSON object only.\n"
  + "Decide if the player is asking HOW TO DO a specific action in the game (build, place, break, fly, sprint, plant a tree, open a door, use a tool, manage inventory, etc.).\n"
  + "- action \"answer\": they ask how to do a specific in-game action the GUIDE covers. Give a SHORT simple answer (max ~180 chars) from the GUIDE and ALWAYS include the control (e.g. right click / tap).\n"
  + "- action \"guide\": ONLY for broad whole-game questions like how do I play, how do I get started, what do I do. Set text to a short nudge to open the How to Play book (top-right).\n"
  + "- action \"none\": EVERYTHING else. This includes greetings, statements, opinions, and questions that merely MENTION game things but do NOT ask how to perform an action. Examples of none: how do you know I have doors, do you like my build, is this cool, why is it laggy, who made this.\n"
  + "Note: how do I build or how do I make stuff = answer (placing blocks). how do I play = guide.\n"
  + "Examples:\n"
  + "Player: how do I place blocks -> {\"action\":\"answer\",\"text\":\"Right click (or tap on mobile) to place a block. It snaps into place.\"}\n"
  + "Player: how do I build -> {\"action\":\"answer\",\"text\":\"Build by placing blocks - right click (or tap on mobile) where you want one and it snaps into place.\"}\n"
  + "Player: how do I open doors -> {\"action\":\"answer\",\"text\":\"Right click a door (tap on mobile) to open or place it.\"}\n"
  + "Player: how do I play -> {\"action\":\"guide\",\"text\":\"Tap the How to Play book at the top-right to learn the basics!\"}\n"
  + "Player: how do you know I have doors? -> {\"action\":\"none\",\"text\":\"\"}\n"
  + "Player: do you like my house -> {\"action\":\"none\",\"text\":\"\"}\n"
  + "Player: this game is laggy -> {\"action\":\"none\",\"text\":\"\"}\n"
  + "Player: hi -> {\"action\":\"none\",\"text\":\"\"}\n"
  + "Reply with ONLY the JSON object, nothing else.\n\nGUIDE:\n";

// Deterministic routing net. Small models frequently miss the JSON action spec,
// so for clearly on-topic how-to questions we map to a canned guide answer (or a
// nudge) instead of going silent. Returns {action,text} or null (off-topic).
async function getHelpGuide(env, target) {
  try {
    const row = await env.DB.prepare("SELECT content FROM help_guide WHERE target = ?").bind(target).first();
    return row && row.content ? row.content : null;
  } catch (err) {
    return null;
  }
}

// The game (HelpGuideSync) posts the in-game How to Play text here so the bot is
// always grounded in the exact guide. Best-effort: a missing table can't break it.
async function handleHelpGuideSync(request, env) {
  const ingest = request.headers.get("X-Ingest-Token");
  if (!ingest || ingest !== env.INGEST_TOKEN) {
    return json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, 401);
  }
  let body;
  try {
    body = await request.json();
  } catch {
    return json({ error: "Invalid JSON" }, 400);
  }
  const target = parseTarget(body.target);
  const content = String(body.content || "").slice(0, 8000);
  if (!content) return json({ error: "Missing content" }, 400);
  try {
    await env.DB.prepare(`
      INSERT INTO help_guide (target, content, updated_at)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?)
      ON CONFLICT(target) DO UPDATE SET content = excluded.content, updated_at = excluded.updated_at
    `).bind(target, content, nowUnix()).run();
    return json({ ok: true, chars: content.length });
  } catch (err) {
    return json({ ok: true, warning: "help_guide table unavailable" });
  }
}

function guideFallback(question) {
  const q = " " + String(question || "").toLowerCase() + " ";
  // Must look like "how do/can/would/to ..." AND not be a meta question that only
  // mentions game things (how do you know..., do you like..., why is..., are you...).
  const howto = /\bhow (do|can|would|to)\b/.test(q) || q.indexOf("how doi") !== -1;
  const meta = /\bdo you (know|think|see|like|have|remember|feel)\b/.test(q)
    || /\bhow do you know\b/.test(q) || /\bwhy (is|are|do|does)\b/.test(q) || /\bare you\b/.test(q);
  if (!howto || meta) return null;
  const has = function () {
    for (let i = 0; i < arguments.length; i++) {
      if (q.indexOf(arguments[i]) !== -1) return true;
    }
    return false;
  };
  if (has("place", "put down", "put block")) return { action: "answer", text: "Right click - or tap on mobile - to place a block. It snaps into place." };
  if (has("build", "make stuff", "make things")) return { action: "answer", text: "Build by placing blocks: right click (or tap on mobile) where you want one and it snaps into place." };
  if (has("break", "destroy", "mine")) return { action: "answer", text: "Hold left click (tap & hold on mobile) on a block to break it; keep holding to break more." };
  if (has(" fly", "flying")) return { action: "answer", text: "Jump twice to fly (or the fly button on mobile). Jump twice again to land." };
  if (has("sprint", "run faster")) return { action: "answer", text: "Hold Ctrl to sprint (or the sprint button on mobile)." };
  if (has("tree", "sapling", "grow", "plant")) return { action: "answer", text: "Big trees (Redwood, Dark Oak) need 4 saplings in a 2x2 square. Other trees need 1 - leave open space above." };
  if (has("inventory", "hotbar")) return { action: "answer", text: "Open your inventory with E (inventory button on mobile), then click/tap a block to add it to your hotbar." };
  if (has("shear", "branch", "vine", "sugar cane", "leaves")) return { action: "answer", text: "Use Shears (right click / tap) to snip leaves into branches, or stop vines and sugar cane from growing." };
  if (has("shovel", "path")) return { action: "answer", text: "Use the Shovel on grass (right click / tap) to turn it into a path block." };
  if (has("open door", "place door", "door")) return { action: "answer", text: "Right click a door (tap on mobile) to place or open it. Doors snap to 6 spots and line up with your wall." };
  if (has("fence")) return { action: "answer", text: "Fences hook onto nearby blocks; right click (tap) a fence to unhook or re-hook it." };
  if (has("frame", "wallpaper")) return { action: "answer", text: "Place a frame, then use it on any solid block (right click / tap) to copy that block's look." };
  if (has("slab")) return { action: "answer", text: "Aim at a block's top or bottom for a flat slab, or a side for a standing slab." };
  if (has("play", "get started", "what do i do", "how to play")) return { action: "guide", text: "Open the How to Play book (top-right) - it walks you through everything!" };
  return null;
}

async function handleChatHelp(request, env) {
  const ingest = request.headers.get("X-Ingest-Token");
  if (!ingest || ingest !== env.INGEST_TOKEN) {
    return json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, 401);
  }

  let body;
  try {
    body = await request.json();
  } catch {
    return json({ error: "Invalid JSON" }, 400);
  }

  const question = String(body.question || "").slice(0, 200).trim();
  if (!question) return json({ action: "none", text: "" });
  if (!env.AI) {
    const net = guideFallback(question);
    return json(net || { action: "none", text: "" });
  }

  const target = parseTarget(body.target);
  const guide = (await getHelpGuide(env, target)) || HELP_GUIDE;
  const out = await aiComplete(env, HELP_PROMPT_PREFIX + guide, "Player: " + question, 256);
  if (out == null) {
    // AI unavailable/errored - deterministic fallback so real how-to questions still work.
    const net = guideFallback(question);
    return json(net || { action: "none", text: "" });
  }

  let parsed = {};
  try {
    const m = String(out).match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
    parsed = m ? JSON.parse(m[0]) : {};
  } catch (err) {
    return json({ action: "none", text: "" });
  }

  let action = ["answer", "guide", "none"].indexOf(parsed.action) !== -1 ? parsed.action : "none";
  let text = String(parsed.text || "").replace(/\s+/g, " ").slice(0, 220).trim();

  // Gemini is the authority on intent. Only patch obviously-broken output - do
  // NOT override a "none" (that is the model correctly judging it is not a how-to).
  if (action === "answer" && !text) {
    const net = guideFallback(question);
    if (net && net.action === "answer") { text = net.text; } else { action = "none"; }
  }
  if (action === "guide" && !text) text = "Open the How to Play book (top-right) and I'll show you!";
  if (action === "none") text = "";
  return json({ action, text });
}

async function handleAdminCommand(request, env) {
  let body;
  try {
    body = await request.json();
  } catch {
    return json({ error: "Invalid JSON" }, 400);
  }

  const { command, payload, target } = body;
  if (!command || typeof command !== "string") {
    return json({ error: "Missing 'command' field" }, 400);
  }

  const targetKey = parseTarget(target);
  const universeId = UNIVERSES[targetKey];
  if (!universeId) {
    return json({ error: `Unknown target '${targetKey}'`, valid: Object.keys(UNIVERSES) }, 400);
  }

  const message = JSON.stringify({
    command,
    payload: payload || {},
    timestamp: Date.now(),
  });

  if (message.length > 1024) {
    return json({ error: "Message exceeds 1KB limit" }, 400);
  }

  const robloxRes = await fetch(
    `https://apis.roblox.com/messaging-service/v1/universes/${universeId}/topics/${TOPIC}`,
    {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "x-api-key": env.ROBLOX_API_KEY,
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ message }),
    },
  );

  if (!robloxRes.ok) {
    const errText = await robloxRes.text();
    return json({
      error: "Roblox API error",
      status: robloxRes.status,
      target: targetKey,
      detail: errText,
    }, 502);
  }

  return json({ success: true, command, target: targetKey, timestamp: Date.now() });
}

/* Dashboard top region: live player list on the left (~58%) with a stacked
   column of at-a-glance metrics on the right, so the wide desktop layout reads
   like an ops dashboard instead of one tall scrolling column. Collapses to a
   single stacked column on narrow viewports. */
.dash-top {
  display: grid; grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr; gap: 16px; margin-bottom: 16px;
  align-items: start;
}
.dash-top > .live-card { margin-bottom: 0; }
.dash-top > .lb-gallery { margin-bottom: 0; }
.dash-side { display: grid; gap: 16px; }
.dash-side > .chart-card { margin-bottom: 0 !important; }

/* Responsive gallery for the leaderboard cards: they sit side by side and
   auto-fit/wrap as the viewport changes — 3-up on wide desktops, 2-up on
   medium, 1-up on phones — so they always resize to fill the row nicely. */
.lb-gallery {
  display: grid;
  grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(320px, 1fr));
  gap: 16px; margin-bottom: 16px; align-items: start;
}
.lb-gallery > .chart-card { margin-bottom: 0 !important; }
.lb-gallery > .gallery-wide { grid-column: 1 / -1; }
@media (max-width: 1100px) { .dash-top { grid-template-columns: 1fr; } }

/* Dense 2-up layout for the stacked full-width charts on desktop. The
   preserveAspectRatio="none" SVGs stretch to fill their column, so two per
   row keeps each chart near its native 600px and fits far more on screen.
   Collapses to a single column on narrow viewports. */
/* Masonry-style columns so mixed-height cards (tall charts vs short funnel
   tiles) pack tightly down each column instead of leaving dead space beside a
   short card. Reads top-to-bottom down column one, then column two. */
.chart-grid {
  column-count: 2; column-gap: 16px; margin-bottom: 0;
}
.chart-grid > .chart-card {
  break-inside: avoid; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;
  margin-bottom: 16px !important; width: 100%;
}
@media (max-width: 900px) { .chart-grid { column-count: 1; } }

<script>
const TOKEN_KEY = "bb_admin_token";
const TARGET_KEY = "bb_admin_target";
const TAB_KEY = "bb_admin_tab";
const tokenInput = document.getElementById("token");
const tokenStatus = document.getElementById("tokenStatus");
const saveTokenBtn = document.getElementById("saveToken");
const targetSelect = document.getElementById("target");
const logEntries = document.getElementById("logEntries");

const savedToken = localStorage.getItem(TOKEN_KEY);
if (savedToken) { tokenInput.value = savedToken; tokenStatus.textContent = "🔓"; }
const savedTarget = localStorage.getItem(TARGET_KEY);
if (savedTarget) targetSelect.value = savedTarget;

saveTokenBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
  const t = tokenInput.value.trim();
  if (t) {
    localStorage.setItem(TOKEN_KEY, t);
    tokenStatus.textContent = "✅";
    setTimeout(() => { tokenStatus.textContent = "🔓"; }, 1000);
  } else {
    localStorage.removeItem(TOKEN_KEY);
    tokenStatus.textContent = "🔒";
  }
});

function updateTargetStyle() {
  targetSelect.classList.remove("prod", "dev");
  targetSelect.classList.add(targetSelect.value);
  localStorage.setItem(TARGET_KEY, targetSelect.value);
  const activeTab = document.querySelector(".tab.active")?.dataset.tab;
  if (activeTab === "analytics") {
    loadAnalytics();
  } else if (activeTab === "gifts") {
    loadGiftOnlineCount();
  } else if (activeTab === "feedback") {
    loadFeedback();
  } else if (activeTab === "players") {
    loadPlayers();
  } else if (activeTab === "economy") {
    loadEconomyTab();
  } else if (activeTab === "chat") {
    loadChat();
  } else if (activeTab === "commands") {
    loadCommandServers();
  }
}
targetSelect.addEventListener("change", updateTargetStyle);
updateTargetStyle();

function activateTab(name) {
  const btn = document.querySelector('.tab[data-tab="' + name + '"]');
  if (!btn) return;
  document.querySelectorAll(".tab").forEach((b) => b.classList.remove("active"));
  document.querySelectorAll(".tabpanel").forEach((p) => p.classList.remove("active"));
  btn.classList.add("active");
  document.querySelector('.tabpanel[data-panel="' + name + '"]').classList.add("active");
  localStorage.setItem(TAB_KEY, name);
  if (name === "analytics") {
    loadAnalytics();
    startLivePolling();
    stopGiftPolling();
  } else if (name === "gifts") {
    stopLivePolling();
    initGifts();
  } else if (name === "feedback") {
    stopLivePolling();
    stopGiftPolling();
    loadFeedback();
  } else if (name === "players") {
    stopLivePolling();
    stopGiftPolling();
    loadPlayers();
  } else if (name === "economy") {
    stopLivePolling();
    stopGiftPolling();
    loadEconomyTab();
  } else if (name === "chat") {
    stopLivePolling();
    stopGiftPolling();
    loadChatTab();
  } else if (name === "commands") {
    stopLivePolling();
    stopGiftPolling();
    loadCommandServers();
  } else {
    stopLivePolling();
    stopGiftPolling();
  }
}

document.querySelectorAll(".tab").forEach((btn) => {
  btn.addEventListener("click", () => activateTab(btn.dataset.tab));
});

// ============================================================================
// Feedback tab
// ============================================================================
let fbFilter = "inbox";

function escapeHtmlFb(s) {
  return String(s == null ? "" : s)
    .replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
    .replace(/"/g, "&quot;");
}

function fbDate(unix) {
  if (!unix) return "";
  try { return new Date(unix * 1000).toLocaleString(); } catch { return ""; }
}

async function loadFeedback() {
  const list = document.getElementById("fb-list");
  if (!list) return;
  const token = (document.getElementById("token").value || "").trim();
  if (!token) {
    list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">Set your admin token, then Refresh.</div>';
    return;
  }
  list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">Loading…</div>';
  try {
    const data = await apiGet("/feedback?filter=" + encodeURIComponent(fbFilter));
    const rows = data.rows || [];
    if (!rows.length) {
      list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No ' +
        (fbFilter === "spam" ? "spam" : "feedback") + ' here.</div>';
      return;
    }
    list.innerHTML = rows.map((r) => {
      const spam = r.spam ? " spam" : "";
      const name = escapeHtmlFb(r.display_name || r.username || "?");
      const handle = r.username ? " (@" + escapeHtmlFb(r.username) + ")" : "";
      const replyHtml = r.reply
        ? '<div class="fb-reply"><span class="fb-reply-label">Your reply · ' +
            escapeHtmlFb(fbDate(r.replied_at)) + '</span>' + escapeHtmlFb(r.reply) + '</div>'
        : "";
      const fbId = escapeHtmlFb(r.feedback_id);
      const btnLabel = r.reply ? "↩ Edit reply" : "↩ Reply";
      const existing = r.reply ? escapeHtmlFb(r.reply) : "";
      const actions =
        '<div class="fb-actions"><button class="fb-reply-btn" data-fbid="' + fbId + '">' +
          btnLabel + '</button></div>' +
        '<div class="fb-reply-box">' +
          '<textarea class="fb-reply-input" maxlength="300" placeholder="Write a reply…">' +
            existing + '</textarea>' +
          '<div class="fb-reply-row">' +
            '<button class="fb-reply-send" data-fbid="' + fbId + '">Send reply</button>' +
            '<button class="fb-reply-cancel">Cancel</button>' +
            '<span class="fb-reply-count"></span>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>';
      return '<div class="fb-item' + spam + '">' +
        '<div class="fb-item-head"><span class="fb-user">' + name + handle + '</span>' +
        '<span class="fb-date">' + escapeHtmlFb(fbDate(r.created_at)) + '</span></div>' +
        '<div class="fb-text">' + escapeHtmlFb(r.text) + '</div>' +
        replyHtml + actions + '</div>';
    }).join("");
  } catch (err) {
    list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">Error: ' + escapeHtmlFb(err.message) + '</div>';
  }
}

document.querySelectorAll(".fb-tab").forEach((btn) => {
  btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    document.querySelectorAll(".fb-tab").forEach((b) => b.classList.remove("active"));
    btn.classList.add("active");
    fbFilter = btn.dataset.fbfilter;
    loadFeedback();
  });
});
const fbRefreshBtn = document.getElementById("fb-refresh");
if (fbRefreshBtn) fbRefreshBtn.addEventListener("click", loadFeedback);

async function sendFeedbackReply(sendBtn) {
  const item = sendBtn.closest(".fb-item");
  if (!item) return;
  const ta = item.querySelector(".fb-reply-input");
  const text = (ta && ta.value || "").trim();
  const feedbackId = sendBtn.dataset.fbid;
  if (!text) { alert("Reply is empty"); return; }
  const token = (document.getElementById("token").value || "").trim();
  if (!token) { alert("Set your admin token first"); return; }
  const target = targetSelect.value;
  sendBtn.disabled = true;
  const orig = sendBtn.textContent;
  sendBtn.textContent = "Sending…";
  try {
    const res = await fetch("/feedback/reply?target=" + encodeURIComponent(target), {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", "X-Admin-Token": token },
      body: JSON.stringify({ feedbackId, text }),
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    if (res.ok && data.success) {
      loadFeedback();
    } else {
      alert("Failed: " + (data.error || res.status));
      sendBtn.disabled = false;
      sendBtn.textContent = orig;
    }
  } catch (err) {
    alert("Error: " + err.message);
    sendBtn.disabled = false;
    sendBtn.textContent = orig;
  }
}

const fbListEl = document.getElementById("fb-list");
if (fbListEl) {
  fbListEl.addEventListener("click", (e) => {
    const replyBtn = e.target.closest(".fb-reply-btn");
    if (replyBtn) {
      const box = replyBtn.closest(".fb-item").querySelector(".fb-reply-box");
      if (box) {
        const opening = !box.classList.contains("open");
        box.classList.toggle("open", opening);
        if (opening) {
          const ta = box.querySelector(".fb-reply-input");
          if (ta) { ta.focus(); ta.setSelectionRange(ta.value.length, ta.value.length); }
        }
      }
      return;
    }
    const cancelBtn = e.target.closest(".fb-reply-cancel");
    if (cancelBtn) {
      const box = cancelBtn.closest(".fb-reply-box");
      if (box) box.classList.remove("open");
      return;
    }
    const sendBtn = e.target.closest(".fb-reply-send");
    if (sendBtn) { sendFeedbackReply(sendBtn); return; }
  });
  fbListEl.addEventListener("input", (e) => {
    const ta = e.target.closest(".fb-reply-input");
    if (!ta) return;
    const counter = ta.closest(".fb-reply-box").querySelector(".fb-reply-count");
    if (counter) counter.textContent = ta.value.length + " / 300";
  });
}

async function loadCommandServers() {
  const selects = document.querySelectorAll(".server-select");
  if (!selects.length) return;
  const token = (tokenInput && tokenInput.value.trim()) || "";
  let servers = [];
  if (token) {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(window.location.origin + "/admin/servers?target=" + encodeURIComponent(targetSelect.value), { headers: { "X-Admin-Token": token } });
      if (res.ok) { const d = await res.json(); servers = d.servers || []; }
    } catch (e) {}
  }
  selects.forEach((sel) => {
    const prev = sel.value;
    sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">All servers</option>';
    servers.forEach((sv) => {
      const opt = document.createElement("option");
      opt.value = sv.serverId;
      const names = (sv.players || []).join(", ");
      opt.textContent = (sv.count || 0) + " player" + ((sv.count === 1) ? "" : "s") + (names ? " — " + names : "") + " [" + String(sv.serverId).slice(0, 8) + "]";
      sel.appendChild(opt);
    });
    if (prev) sel.value = prev;
  });
}

if (typeof tokenInput !== "undefined" && tokenInput) {
  tokenInput.addEventListener("change", () => {
    const at = document.querySelector(".tab.active");
    if (at && at.dataset.tab === "commands") loadCommandServers();
  });
}

function buildPayload(cmd) {
  switch (cmd) {
    case "broadcast": {
      const msg = document.getElementById("bc-message").value.trim();
      if (!msg) { alert("Message required"); return null; }
      const targetJobId = (document.getElementById("bc-server") || {}).value || undefined;
      return { message: msg, targetJobId };
    }
    case "pin": {
      const msg = document.getElementById("pin-message").value.trim();
      if (!msg) { alert("Message required"); return null; }
      const color = document.getElementById("pin-color").value;
      const label = document.getElementById("pin-label").value;
      const targetJobId = (document.getElementById("pin-server") || {}).value || undefined;
      return { message: msg, color, label, targetJobId };
    }
    case "unpin":
      return {};
    case "setonce": {
      const msg = document.getElementById("once-message").value.trim();
      if (!msg) { alert("Message required"); return null; }
      const color = document.getElementById("once-color").value;
      const label = document.getElementById("once-label").value;
      return { message: msg, color, label, onceId: Date.now() };
    }
    case "clearonce":
      return {};
    case "softupdate":
      return { reason: document.getElementById("su-reason").value.trim() || undefined };
    case "urgentupdate":
      return { reason: document.getElementById("uu-reason").value.trim() || undefined };
    case "kick": {
      const username = document.getElementById("k-username").value.trim();
      if (!username) { alert("Username required"); return null; }
      const reason = document.getElementById("k-reason").value.trim();
      return { username, reason: reason || undefined };
    }
    case "ban": {
      const username = document.getElementById("b-username").value.trim();
      if (!username) { alert("Username required"); return null; }
      const reason = document.getElementById("b-reason").value.trim();
      const duration = Number.parseInt(document.getElementById("b-duration").value, 10);
      return { username, reason: reason || undefined, duration };
    }
  }
  return {};
}

function addLogEntry(text, cls) {
  const empty = logEntries.querySelector(".log-entry.empty");
  if (empty) empty.remove();
  const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit", second: "2-digit" });
  const entry = document.createElement("div");
  entry.className = "log-entry " + (cls || "");
  const timeSpan = document.createElement("span");
  timeSpan.className = "time";
  timeSpan.textContent = time;
  const textSpan = document.createElement("span");
  textSpan.className = "text";
  textSpan.textContent = text;
  entry.appendChild(timeSpan);
  entry.appendChild(textSpan);
  logEntries.insertBefore(entry, logEntries.firstChild);
  while (logEntries.children.length > 30) logEntries.lastChild.remove();
  return entry;
}

async function sendCommand(cmd) {
  const token = tokenInput.value.trim();
  if (!token) { alert("Set your admin token first"); return; }
  const payload = buildPayload(cmd);
  if (payload === null) return;
  const target = targetSelect.value;
  const label = cmd + " → " + target.toUpperCase();
  const pending = addLogEntry("dispatching " + label, "pending");
  try {
    const res = await fetch(window.location.origin, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", "X-Admin-Token": token },
      body: JSON.stringify({ command: cmd, target, payload }),
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    if (pending) pending.remove();
    if (res.ok && data.success) addLogEntry("✓ " + label, "success");
    else addLogEntry("✗ " + label + " — " + (data.error || res.status), "error");
  } catch (err) {
    if (pending) pending.remove();
    addLogEntry("✗ " + label + " — " + err.message, "error");
  }
}

document.querySelectorAll("button[data-cmd]").forEach((btn) => {
  btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
    const cmd = btn.dataset.cmd;
    const confirmText = btn.dataset.confirm;
    if (confirmText && !confirm(confirmText)) return;
    sendCommand(cmd);
  });
});

const liveContent = document.getElementById("liveContent");
const refreshLiveBtn = document.getElementById("refreshLive");

let dailyDays = 30;

let sessionLengthDays = 30;
let plusDays = 30;

function setupRangeButtons(selector, setter, loader) {
  document.querySelectorAll(selector + " button").forEach((btn) => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
      document.querySelectorAll(selector + " button").forEach((b) => b.classList.remove("active"));
      btn.classList.add("active");
      setter(Number.parseInt(btn.dataset.days, 10));
      loader();
    });
  });
}

setupRangeButtons("#dailyRange", (v) => { dailyDays = v; }, loadDaily);

refreshLiveBtn.addEventListener("click", loadLive);

const LIVE_REFRESH_INTERVAL_MS = 15000;
let livePollTimer = null;
let livePollInFlight = false;
let liveManuallyPaused = false;
const livePulse = document.getElementById("livePulse");
const livePulseText = document.getElementById("livePulseText");
const pauseLiveBtn = document.getElementById("pauseLive");

function setPulseState(state) {
  livePulse.classList.toggle("paused", state !== "live");
  if (state === "live") {
    livePulseText.textContent = "live";
    pauseLiveBtn.textContent = "⏸";
    pauseLiveBtn.title = "Pause auto-refresh";
  } else if (state === "paused") {
    livePulseText.textContent = "paused";
    pauseLiveBtn.textContent = "▶";
    pauseLiveBtn.title = "Resume auto-refresh";
  } else {
    livePulseText.textContent = "idle";
    pauseLiveBtn.textContent = "⏸";
  }
}

async function pollLive() {
  if (livePollInFlight) return;
  if (!tokenInput.value.trim()) return;

  livePollInFlight = true;
  try {
    const data = await apiGet("/stats/live");
    renderLive(data);
    document.getElementById("kpi-live").textContent = data.playerCount;
    document.getElementById("kpi-live-sub").textContent = "across " + data.serverCount + " server" + (data.serverCount === 1 ? "" : "s");
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn("pollLive:", err.message);
  } finally {
    livePollInFlight = false;
  }
}

function startLivePolling() {
  if (livePollTimer || liveManuallyPaused) return;
  if (document.hidden) return;
  if (document.querySelector(".tab.active")?.dataset.tab !== "analytics") return;
  setPulseState("live");
  pollLive();
  livePollTimer = setInterval(pollLive, LIVE_REFRESH_INTERVAL_MS);
}

function stopLivePolling(reason) {
  if (livePollTimer) {
    clearInterval(livePollTimer);
    livePollTimer = null;
  }
  setPulseState(reason || "paused");
}

pauseLiveBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
  if (liveManuallyPaused) {
    liveManuallyPaused = false;
    startLivePolling();
  } else {
    liveManuallyPaused = true;
    stopLivePolling("paused");
  }
});

document.addEventListener("visibilitychange", () => {
  if (document.hidden) {
    if (livePollTimer) {
      clearInterval(livePollTimer);
      livePollTimer = null;
    }
    setPulseState("hidden");
  } else {
    startLivePolling();
  }
});

async function apiGet(path) {
  const token = tokenInput.value.trim();
  if (!token) throw new Error("No admin token set");
  const target = targetSelect.value;
  const sep = path.includes("?") ? "&" : "?";
  const res = await fetch(path + sep + "target=" + encodeURIComponent(target), {
    headers: { "X-Admin-Token": token },
  });
  if (!res.ok) {
    const txt = await res.text();
    throw new Error("HTTP " + res.status + " — " + txt);
  }
  return res.json();
}

async function loadLive() {
  refreshLiveBtn.disabled = true;
  refreshLiveBtn.textContent = "loading…";
  try {
    const data = await apiGet("/stats/live");
    renderLive(data);
    document.getElementById("kpi-live").textContent = data.playerCount;
    document.getElementById("kpi-live-sub").textContent = "across " + data.serverCount + " server" + (data.serverCount === 1 ? "" : "s");
  } catch (err) {
    liveContent.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">Error: ' + escapeHtml(err.message) + '</div>';
  } finally {
    refreshLiveBtn.disabled = false;
    refreshLiveBtn.textContent = "↻ Refresh";
  }
}

let lastLiveData = null;

const thumbCache = new Map();

async function hydrateAvatars() {
  const imgs = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#liveContent img.avatar[data-uid]'));
  const need = [];
  for (const img of imgs) {
    const uid = img.getAttribute("data-uid");
    if (thumbCache.has(uid)) {
      if (!img.src) img.src = thumbCache.get(uid);
    } else if (!need.includes(uid)) {
      need.push(uid);
    }
  }
  if (!need.length) return;
  const chunks = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < need.length; i += 100) chunks.push(need.slice(i, i + 100));
  try {
    await Promise.all(chunks.map(async (chunk) => {
      const data = await apiGet("/thumbnails?userIds=" + encodeURIComponent(chunk.join(",")));
      const map = data.thumbnails || {};
      for (const uid in map) thumbCache.set(uid, map[uid]);
    }));
    for (const img of imgs) {
      const uid = img.getAttribute("data-uid");
      if (!img.src && thumbCache.has(uid)) img.src = thumbCache.get(uid);
    }
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn("hydrateAvatars:", err.message);
  }
}

function formatPlayTime(seconds) {
  if (!seconds || seconds < 60) return (seconds || 0) + "s";
  if (seconds < 3600) return Math.floor(seconds / 60) + "m";
  const h = Math.floor(seconds / 3600);
  const m = Math.floor((seconds % 3600) / 60);
  return h + "h " + m + "m";
}

function streakBadge(n) {
  if (!n || n <= 0) return '<span style="color:var(--text-faint)">—</span>';
  let cls = "info";
  if (n >= 7) cls = "new";
  else if (n >= 3) cls = "warning";
  return '<span class="pill ' + cls + '">🔥 ' + n + '</span>';
}

function renderCoinDistribution(data) {
  const content = document.getElementById("coinDistContent");
  if (!content) return;
  const meta = document.getElementById("coinDistMeta");
  const players = (data && data.players) || [];
  if (!players.length) {
    content.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No players online</div>';
    if (meta) meta.textContent = "";
    return;
  }

  // Buckets aligned to the economy's pricing tiers (cheap packs ~750, save slot
  // ~1000, standard packs 1.2k–1.5k, mods 2k–2.5k) so you can read sink pressure.
  const buckets = [
    { label: "0", min: 0, max: 0 },
    { label: "1–499", min: 1, max: 499 },
    { label: "500–999", min: 500, max: 999 },
    { label: "1k–1,999", min: 1000, max: 1999 },
    { label: "2k–3,999", min: 2000, max: 3999 },
    { label: "4k–7,999", min: 4000, max: 7999 },
    { label: "8,000+", min: 8000, max: Infinity },
  ];
  const counts = buckets.map(() => 0);
  let sum = 0;
  const all = [];
  for (const p of players) {
    const c = p.coins || 0;
    sum += c;
    all.push(c);
    for (let i = 0; i < buckets.length; i++) {
      if (c >= buckets[i].min && c <= buckets[i].max) { counts[i]++; break; }
    }
  }
  const total = players.length;
  const maxCount = Math.max(1, ...counts);
  all.sort((a, b) => a - b);
  const mid = Math.floor(all.length / 2);
  const median = all.length % 2 ? all[mid] : Math.round((all[mid - 1] + all[mid]) / 2);
  if (meta) meta.textContent = "median " + median.toLocaleString() + " · avg " + Math.round(sum / total).toLocaleString() + " · " + total + " online";

  let html = '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px">';
  buckets.forEach((b, i) => {
    const barPct = (counts[i] / maxCount) * 100;
    const sharePct = Math.round((counts[i] / total) * 100);
    html += '<div style="position:relative;display:grid;grid-template-columns:84px 1fr auto;gap:10px;align-items:center;padding:7px 12px;background:var(--bg-input);border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;font-size:13px">'
      + '<div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;bottom:0;width:' + barPct.toFixed(1) + '%;background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--success-glow),transparent);border-left:2px solid var(--success);border-radius:8px 0 0 8px;pointer-events:none"></div>'
      + '<div style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);z-index:1">' + b.label + '</div>'
      + '<div></div>'
      + '<div style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:12px;color:var(--text);z-index:1">' + counts[i] + ' <span style="color:var(--text-dim)">(' + sharePct + '%)</span></div>'
      + '</div>';
  });
  html += '</div>';
  content.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderLive(data) {
  lastLiveData = data;
  renderCoinDistribution(data);
  if (!data.players || data.players.length === 0) {
    const reason = data.serverCount === 0 ? "(no servers reporting in the last 60s)" : "";
    liveContent.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No players online ' + reason + '</div>';
    return;
  }

  const sortBy = document.getElementById("sortBy").value;
  const sorted = data.players.slice();
  sorted.sort((a, b) => {
    switch (sortBy) {
      case "playTime": return (b.playTime || 0) - (a.playTime || 0);
      case "streak": return (b.streak || 0) - (a.streak || 0);
      case "coins": return (b.coins || 0) - (a.coins || 0);
      case "likes": return (b.likes || 0) - (a.likes || 0);
      case "username": return String(a.username).localeCompare(String(b.username));
      case "isNew": return (b.isNew ? 1 : 0) - (a.isNew ? 1 : 0);
      default: return 0;
    }
  });

  const summary = '<div class="player-count-summary">Showing ' + sorted.length + ' player' + (sorted.length === 1 ? "" : "s") + ' across ' + data.serverCount + ' server' + (data.serverCount === 1 ? "" : "s") + '</div>';

  // Phones: stacked cards (stats on top, type + Join on a second line) so the list
  // never scrolls sideways. Desktop keeps the full table below.
  if (window.matchMedia("(max-width: 640px)").matches) {
    liveContent.innerHTML = renderLiveCards(sorted, data) + summary;
    hydrateAvatars();
    return;
  }

  let html = '<div class="player-table-wrap"><table class="player-table"><thead><tr>';
  html += '<th></th><th>Player</th><th>Play Time</th><th>Streak</th><th>Coins</th><th>Likes</th><th>Type</th><th>Server</th><th>Join</th>';
  html += '</tr></thead><tbody>';

  for (const p of sorted) {
    const newPill = p.isNew ? '<span class="pill new">NEW</span>' : '<span class="pill info">Returning</span>';
    html += '<tr>';
    html += '<td><img class="avatar" data-uid="' + escapeHtml(p.userId) + '"' + (thumbCache.get(String(p.userId)) ? ' src="' + thumbCache.get(String(p.userId)) + '"' : '') + ' alt=""></td>';
    html += '<td><div class="username">' + escapeHtml(p.username) + '</div><div class="userid">' + escapeHtml(p.userId) + '</div></td>';
    html += '<td>' + formatPlayTime(p.playTime) + '</td>';
    html += '<td>' + streakBadge(p.streak) + '</td>';
    html += '<td>' + (p.coins || 0).toLocaleString() + '</td>';
    html += '<td>' + (p.likes || 0) + '</td>';
    html += '<td>' + newPill + '</td>';
    html += '<td class="server">' + escapeHtml((p.serverId || "").slice(0, 8)) + '</td>';
    html += '<td>' + (data.placeId ? '<a class="join-btn" href="roblox://experiences/start?placeId=' + encodeURIComponent(data.placeId) + '&gameInstanceId=' + encodeURIComponent(p.serverId || "") + '">Join</a>' : '<span style="color:var(--text-faint)">—</span>') + '</td>';
    html += '</tr>';
  }

  html += '</tbody></table></div>';
  html += summary;
  liveContent.innerHTML = html;
  hydrateAvatars();
}

function renderLiveCards(sorted, data) {
  let html = '<div class="player-cards">';
  for (const p of sorted) {
    const newPill = p.isNew ? '<span class="pill new">NEW</span>' : '<span class="pill info">Returning</span>';
    const join = data.placeId
      ? '<a class="join-btn" href="roblox://experiences/start?placeId=' + encodeURIComponent(data.placeId) + '&gameInstanceId=' + encodeURIComponent(p.serverId || "") + '">Join</a>'
      : '<span style="color:var(--text-faint)">—</span>';
    const src = thumbCache.get(String(p.userId));
    html += '<div class="player-card">'
      + '<img class="avatar" data-uid="' + escapeHtml(p.userId) + '"' + (src ? ' src="' + src + '"' : '') + ' alt="">'
      + '<div class="pc-main">'
        + '<div class="pc-top">'
          + '<div class="pc-id"><div class="username">' + escapeHtml(p.username) + '</div><div class="userid">' + escapeHtml(p.userId) + '</div></div>'
          + newPill
        + '</div>'
        + '<div class="pc-stats">'
          + '<span>⏱ <b>' + formatPlayTime(p.playTime) + '</b></span>'
          + '<span>🔥 <b>' + (p.streak || 0) + '</b></span>'
          + '<span>🪙 <b>' + (p.coins || 0).toLocaleString() + '</b></span>'
          + '<span>❤ <b>' + (p.likes || 0) + '</b></span>'
        + '</div>'
        + '<div class="pc-actions">' + join + '</div>'
      + '</div>'
    + '</div>';
  }
  html += '</div>';
  return html;
}

document.getElementById("sortBy").addEventListener("change", () => {
  if (lastLiveData) renderLive(lastLiveData);
});

window.matchMedia("(max-width: 640px)").addEventListener("change", () => {
  if (lastLiveData) renderLive(lastLiveData);
});

async function safeLoad(name, path, render) {
  try {
    render(await apiGet(path));
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(name + ":", err);
  }
}

async function loadDaily() {
  return safeLoad("loadDaily", "/stats/daily?days=" + dailyDays, (data) => {
    renderStackedBarChart("dailyChart", data.rows || []);

    const today = new Date((Date.now() / 1000 + -300 * 60) * 1000).toISOString().slice(0, 10); // local Central; mirror TZ_OFFSET_MIN in worker
    const todayRow = (data.rows || []).find((r) => r.date === today);
    document.getElementById("kpi-today").textContent = todayRow ? ((todayRow.new_count || 0) + (todayRow.returning_count || 0)) : 0;
    if (todayRow) {
      document.getElementById("kpi-today-sub").textContent = (todayRow.new_count || 0) + " new · " + (todayRow.returning_count || 0) + " returning";
    }
    const last7 = (data.rows || []).slice(-7);
    const new7 = last7.reduce((a, r) => a + (r.new_count || 0), 0);
    document.getElementById("kpi-7d-new").textContent = new7;
  });
}

  return safeLoad("loadConcurrency", "/stats/concurrency?days=" + concurrencyDays, (data) => renderLineChart("concurrencyChart", data.rows || []));
}

  return safeLoad("loadDailyPeak", "/stats/daily-peak?days=" + dailyPeakDays, (data) => renderDailyPeakChart("dailyPeakChart", data.rows || []));
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Shared chart primitives. Every time-series chart below is 600x200 with a 4-step
// y-axis, date labels along the bottom, and an optional swatch legend in the top
// right. These helpers emit the repeated SVG so each chart only describes what is
// unique about it (its series, colors, and tooltip rows).
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
function chartGeom(padL) {
  const W = 600, H = 200, padR = 12, padT = 12, padB = 30;
  return { W, H, padL, padR, padT, padB, plotW: W - padL - padR, plotH: H - padT - padB };
}

function chartEmpty(svg, rows, msg) {
  if (rows.length) return false;
  svg.innerHTML = '<text x="300" y="100" fill="#4a5170" text-anchor="middle" font-family="JetBrains Mono" font-size="12">' + msg + '</text>';
  return true;
}

function chartGrid(max, g, suffix) {
  let s = "";
  const yTicks = 4;
  for (let i = 0; i <= yTicks; i++) {
    const y = g.padT + g.plotH - (i / yTicks) * g.plotH;
    const v = Math.round((i / yTicks) * max);
    s += '<line x1="' + g.padL + '" y1="' + y + '" x2="' + (g.W - g.padR) + '" y2="' + y + '" stroke="#1f2740" stroke-width="1"/>';
    s += '<text x="' + (g.padL - 6) + '" y="' + (y + 3) + '" fill="#4a5170" text-anchor="end" font-family="JetBrains Mono" font-size="9">' + v + (suffix || "") + '</text>';
  }
  return s;
}

function chartXLabels(rows, g, xOf) {
  let s = "";
  const labelCount = Math.min(6, rows.length);
  for (let i = 0; i < labelCount; i++) {
    const idx = Math.floor(i * (rows.length - 1) / Math.max(1, labelCount - 1));
    const x = xOf(idx);
    const label = (rows[idx].date || "").slice(5);
    s += '<text x="' + x + '" y="' + (g.H - 10) + '" fill="#4a5170" text-anchor="middle" font-family="JetBrains Mono" font-size="9">' + label + '</text>';
  }
  return s;
}

function chartLegend(entries) {
  let s = "";
  for (const e of entries) {
    s += '<rect x="' + e.x + '" y="4" width="8" height="8" fill="' + e.color + '"/><text x="' + (e.x + 12) + '" y="11" fill="#7a83a0" font-family="JetBrains Mono" font-size="9">' + e.label + '</text>';
  }
  return s;
}

// Single-series filled area chart (peak concurrency, session length).
function renderAreaChart(svgId, rows, opt) {
  const svg = document.getElementById(svgId);
  svg.innerHTML = "";
  if (chartEmpty(svg, rows, opt.emptyMsg)) return;
  const g = chartGeom(opt.padL);
  const values = rows.map(opt.valueOf);
  const max = Math.max(1, ...values);
  svg.innerHTML += chartGrid(max, g, opt.suffix);

  const pts = values.map((v, i) => {
    const x = g.padL + (i / Math.max(1, rows.length - 1)) * g.plotW;
    const y = g.padT + g.plotH - (v / max) * g.plotH;
    return [x, y];
  });

  let fillPath = "M " + pts[0][0] + " " + (g.padT + g.plotH);
  pts.forEach((p) => { fillPath += " L " + p[0] + " " + p[1]; });
  fillPath += " L " + pts[pts.length - 1][0] + " " + (g.padT + g.plotH) + " Z";
  svg.innerHTML += '<path d="' + fillPath + '" fill="url(#' + opt.gradId + ')" opacity="0.3"/>';
  svg.innerHTML += '<defs><linearGradient id="' + opt.gradId + '" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1"><stop offset="0%" stop-color="' + opt.color + '"/><stop offset="100%" stop-color="' + opt.color + '" stop-opacity="0"/></linearGradient></defs>';

  let linePath = "M " + pts[0][0] + " " + pts[0][1];
  pts.forEach((p, i) => { if (i > 0) linePath += " L " + p[0] + " " + p[1]; });
  svg.innerHTML += '<path d="' + linePath + '" fill="none" stroke="' + opt.color + '" stroke-width="2" stroke-linejoin="round"/>';

  pts.forEach((p, i) => {
    svg.innerHTML += '<circle cx="' + p[0] + '" cy="' + p[1] + '" r="2.5" fill="' + opt.color + '"><title>' + opt.titleOf(rows[i], values[i], i) + '</title></circle>';
  });

  svg.innerHTML += chartXLabels(rows, g, (idx) => g.padL + (idx / Math.max(1, rows.length - 1)) * g.plotW);

  const points = rows.map((r, i) => ({
    x: pts[i][0],
    markerY: pts[i][1],
    markerColor: opt.color,
    label: r.date,
    entries: opt.entriesOf(r, values[i], i),
  }));
  attachChartTooltip(svgId, points);
}

// Multiple overlaid lines sharing one y-axis (DAU/WAU/MAU, earned/spent).
function renderMultiLineChart(svgId, rows, opt) {
  const svg = document.getElementById(svgId);
  svg.innerHTML = "";
  if (chartEmpty(svg, rows, opt.emptyMsg)) return;
  const g = chartGeom(opt.padL);
  const max = Math.max(1, ...rows.map(opt.maxOf));
  svg.innerHTML += chartGrid(max, g, "");

  const xFor = (i) => g.padL + (i / Math.max(1, rows.length - 1)) * g.plotW;
  const yFor = (v) => g.padT + g.plotH - (v / max) * g.plotH;

  for (const s of opt.series) {
    const pts = rows.map((r, i) => [xFor(i), yFor(r[s.key] || 0)]);
    let linePath = "M " + pts[0][0] + " " + pts[0][1];
    pts.forEach((p, i) => { if (i > 0) linePath += " L " + p[0] + " " + p[1]; });
    svg.innerHTML += '<path d="' + linePath + '" fill="none" stroke="' + s.color + '" stroke-width="2" stroke-linejoin="round"/>';
    pts.forEach((p) => {
      svg.innerHTML += '<circle cx="' + p[0] + '" cy="' + p[1] + '" r="2" fill="' + s.color + '"/>';
    });
  }

  svg.innerHTML += chartXLabels(rows, g, xFor);
  svg.innerHTML += chartLegend(opt.legend);

  const points = rows.map((r, i) => ({
    x: xFor(i),
    markerY: yFor(opt.markerOf(r)),
    markerColor: opt.markerColor,
    label: r.date,
    entries: opt.entriesOf(r),
  }));
  attachChartTooltip(svgId, points);
}

// Bars for one metric with a line overlaid for another (Plus taps/subscribes,
// shop opens/purchases).
function renderBarLineChart(svgId, rows, opt) {
  const svg = document.getElementById(svgId);
  svg.innerHTML = "";
  if (chartEmpty(svg, rows, opt.emptyMsg)) return;
  const g = chartGeom(opt.padL);
  const lineVals = rows.map(opt.lineOf);
  const max = Math.max(1, ...lineVals);
  const step = g.plotW / rows.length;
  const barW = step * 0.5;
  svg.innerHTML += chartGrid(max, g, "");

  rows.forEach((r, i) => {
    const buys = opt.barOf(r);
    if (buys <= 0) return;
    const h = (buys / max) * g.plotH;
    const x = g.padL + i * step + (step - barW) / 2;
    svg.innerHTML += '<rect x="' + x + '" y="' + (g.padT + g.plotH - h) + '" width="' + barW + '" height="' + h + '" fill="' + opt.barColor + '" rx="1"><title>' + opt.barTitle(r, buys) + '</title></rect>';
  });

  const pts = rows.map((r, i) => {
    const x = g.padL + i * step + step / 2;
    const y = g.padT + g.plotH - (lineVals[i] / max) * g.plotH;
    return [x, y];
  });
  let linePath = "M " + pts[0][0] + " " + pts[0][1];
  pts.forEach((p, i) => { if (i > 0) linePath += " L " + p[0] + " " + p[1]; });
  svg.innerHTML += '<path d="' + linePath + '" fill="none" stroke="' + opt.lineColor + '" stroke-width="2" stroke-linejoin="round"/>';
  pts.forEach((p, i) => {
    svg.innerHTML += '<circle cx="' + p[0] + '" cy="' + p[1] + '" r="2.5" fill="' + opt.lineColor + '"><title>' + opt.lineTitle(rows[i], lineVals[i]) + '</title></circle>';
  });

  svg.innerHTML += chartXLabels(rows, g, (idx) => g.padL + idx * step + step / 2);
  svg.innerHTML += chartLegend(opt.legend);

  const points = rows.map((r, i) => ({
    x: pts[i][0],
    markerY: pts[i][1],
    markerColor: opt.lineColor,
    label: r.date,
    entries: opt.entriesOf(r),
  }));
  attachChartTooltip(svgId, points);
}

function renderDailyPeakChart(svgId, rows) {
  renderAreaChart(svgId, rows, {
    emptyMsg: "no data yet",
    padL: 40,
    suffix: "",
    color: "#c97ad9",
    gradId: "peakGrad",
    valueOf: (r) => r.peak || 0,
    titleOf: (r, v) => r.date + ': ' + v + ' players at once',
    entriesOf: (r, v) => {
      const entries = [{ name: r.tracked ? "Peak online" : "Peak (est.)", value: v, color: "#c97ad9" }];
      if (r.tracked && r.servers != null) entries.push({ name: "Servers", value: r.servers, color: null });
      return entries;
    },
  });
}

function renderSessionLengthChart(svgId, rows) {

    emptyMsg: "no completed sessions yet",
