    suffix: "m",
    color: "#5fc97a",
    gradId: "sessionGrad",
    valueOf: (r) => (r.avg_seconds || 0) / 60,
    titleOf: (r, v) => r.date + ': ' + Math.round(v) + 'm avg (' + r.session_count + ' sessions)',
    entriesOf: (r, v) => [
      { name: "Avg length", value: Math.round(v) + "m", color: "#5fc97a" },
      { name: "Sessions", value: r.session_count || 0, color: null },
    ],
  });
}

async function loadPlus() {
  return safeLoad("loadPlus", "/stats/plus?days=" + plusDays, (data) => renderPlus(data));
}

function renderPlus(data) {
  const taps = data.taps || 0;
  const unique = data.uniqueTappers || 0;
  const prospects = data.prospectTaps || 0;
  const buys = data.originPurchases || 0;
  const totalPurchases = data.purchases || 0;
  const conv = data.conversionRate || 0;

  document.getElementById("plus-taps").textContent = taps.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("plus-taps-sub").textContent = "unique: " + unique.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("plus-prospects").textContent = prospects.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("plus-buys").textContent = buys.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("plus-buys-sub").textContent = "of " + totalPurchases.toLocaleString() + " total purchase" + (totalPurchases === 1 ? "" : "s");

  const prospectsPct = taps > 0 ? (prospects / taps) * 100 : 0;
  const buysPct = taps > 0 ? (buys / taps) * 100 : 0;
  document.getElementById("plus-prospects-bar").style.width = prospectsPct.toFixed(1) + "%";
  document.getElementById("plus-buys-bar").style.width = buysPct.toFixed(1) + "%";

  const convEl = document.getElementById("plusConv");
  convEl.textContent = conv + "% tap → subscribe";
  convEl.style.color = conv >= 5 ? "var(--success)" : conv >= 1 ? "var(--warning)" : "var(--text-dim)";

  renderPlusChart("plusChart", data.rows || []);

  const srcEl = document.getElementById("plusSources");
  const sources = data.sources || [];
  if (!sources.length) {
    srcEl.innerHTML = "";
  } else {
    const labelMap = { hud_button: "HUD button", title_screen: "Title screen", unknown: "Unknown" };
    let html = '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap;font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim)">';
    for (const s of sources) {
      const label = labelMap[s.source] || s.source;
      html += '<span class="pill info">' + escapeHtml(label) + ': ' + (s.count || 0).toLocaleString() + '</span>';
    }
    html += '</div>';
    srcEl.innerHTML = html;
  }
}

function renderPlusChart(svgId, rows) {
  renderBarLineChart(svgId, rows, {
    emptyMsg: "no Plus activity yet",
    padL: 40,
    lineOf: (r) => r.taps || 0,
    barOf: (r) => r.purchases || 0,
    barColor: "#5fc97a",
    barTitle: (r, buys) => r.date + ': ' + buys + ' subscribed in-game',
    lineColor: "#5bb0ff",
    lineTitle: (r, v) => r.date + ': ' + v + ' taps',
    legend: [
      { x: 600 - 150, color: "#5bb0ff", label: "taps" },
      { x: 600 - 100, color: "#5fc97a", label: "subscribed" },
    ],
    entriesOf: (r) => [
      { name: "Taps", value: r.taps || 0, color: "#5bb0ff" },
      { name: "Subscribed", value: r.purchases || 0, color: "#5fc97a" },
    ],
  });
}

async function loadEconomy() {
  return safeLoad("loadEconomy", "/stats/economy?days=" + economyDays, (data) => renderEconomy(data));
}

function renderEconomy(data) {
  const earned = data.earned || 0;
  const spent = data.spent || 0;
  const net = data.net || 0;

  document.getElementById("econ-earned").textContent = earned.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("econ-spent").textContent = spent.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("econ-spent-bar").style.width =
    (earned > 0 ? Math.min(100, (spent / earned) * 100) : 0).toFixed(1) + "%";

  const netEl = document.getElementById("econNet");
  const sign = net >= 0 ? "+" : "";
  netEl.textContent = sign + net.toLocaleString() + " net";
  netEl.style.color = net > 0 ? "var(--warning)" : "var(--success)";

  renderEconomyChart("economyChart", data.rows || []);

  const srcEl = document.getElementById("econSources");
  const sources = data.sources || [];
  if (!sources.length) {
    srcEl.innerHTML = "";
  } else {
    let html = '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap;font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:11px">';
    for (const s of sources) {
      const cls = s.direction === "earn" ? "new" : "warning";
      const arrow = s.direction === "earn" ? "+" : "−";
      html += '<span class="pill ' + cls + '">' + arrow + ' ' + escapeHtml(s.source) + ': ' + (s.total || 0).toLocaleString() + '</span>';
    }
    html += '</div>';
    srcEl.innerHTML = html;
  }
}

function renderEconomyChart(svgId, rows) {
  renderMultiLineChart(svgId, rows, {
    emptyMsg: "no coin activity yet",
    padL: 48,
    maxOf: (r) => Math.max(r.earned || 0, r.spent || 0),
    series: [
      { key: "earned", color: "#5bb0ff" },
      { key: "spent", color: "#ffc266" },
    ],
    legend: [
      { x: 600 - 150, color: "#5bb0ff", label: "earned" },
      { x: 600 - 90, color: "#ffc266", label: "spent" },
    ],
    markerColor: "#5bb0ff",
    markerOf: (r) => Math.max(r.earned || 0, r.spent || 0),
    entriesOf: (r) => [
      { name: "Earned", value: (r.earned || 0).toLocaleString(), color: "#5bb0ff" },
      { name: "Spent", value: (r.spent || 0).toLocaleString(), color: "#ffc266" },
      { name: "Net", value: ((r.earned || 0) - (r.spent || 0)).toLocaleString(), color: null },
    ],
  });
}

async function loadActive() {
  return safeLoad("loadActive", "/stats/active?days=" + activeDays, (data) => renderActive(data));
}

function renderActive(data) {
  const c = data.current || { dau: 0, wau: 0, mau: 0, stickiness: 0 };
  document.getElementById("active-dau").textContent = (c.dau || 0).toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("active-wau").textContent = (c.wau || 0).toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("active-mau").textContent = (c.mau || 0).toLocaleString();

  const mau = c.mau || 0;
  document.getElementById("active-dau-bar").style.width = (mau > 0 ? (c.dau / mau) * 100 : 0).toFixed(1) + "%";
  document.getElementById("active-wau-bar").style.width = (mau > 0 ? (c.wau / mau) * 100 : 0).toFixed(1) + "%";

  const stick = document.getElementById("activeStick");
  stick.textContent = (c.stickiness || 0) + "% stickiness (DAU/MAU)";
  stick.style.color = c.stickiness >= 20 ? "var(--success)" : c.stickiness >= 10 ? "var(--warning)" : "var(--text-dim)";

  renderActiveChart("activeChart", data.rows || []);
}

function renderActiveChart(svgId, rows) {
  // Draw widest series first so the daily line sits on top.
  renderMultiLineChart(svgId, rows, {
    emptyMsg: "no data yet",
    padL: 40,
    maxOf: (r) => r.mau || 0,
    series: [
      { key: "mau", color: "#c97ad9" },
      { key: "wau", color: "#5fc97a" },
      { key: "dau", color: "#5bb0ff" },
    ],
    legend: [
      { x: 600 - 180, color: "#5bb0ff", label: "DAU" },
      { x: 600 - 125, color: "#5fc97a", label: "WAU" },
      { x: 600 - 70, color: "#c97ad9", label: "MAU" },
    ],
    markerColor: "#c97ad9",
    markerOf: (r) => r.mau || 0,
    entriesOf: (r) => [
      { name: "DAU", value: (r.dau || 0).toLocaleString(), color: "#5bb0ff" },
      { name: "WAU", value: (r.wau || 0).toLocaleString(), color: "#5fc97a" },
      { name: "MAU", value: (r.mau || 0).toLocaleString(), color: "#c97ad9" },
      { name: "Stickiness", value: (r.stickiness || 0) + "%", color: null },
    ],
  });
}

async function loadShop() {
  return safeLoad("loadShop", "/stats/shop?days=" + shopDays, (data) => renderShop(data));
}

function renderShop(data) {
  const opens = data.opens || 0;
  const purchases = data.purchases || 0;
  const revenue = data.revenue || 0;
  const conv = data.conversionRate || 0;

  document.getElementById("shop-opens").textContent = opens.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("shop-opens-sub").textContent = "unique: " + (data.uniqueOpeners || 0).toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("shop-purchases").textContent = purchases.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("shop-revenue").textContent = "R$ " + revenue.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("shop-purchases-bar").style.width = (opens > 0 ? (purchases / opens) * 100 : 0).toFixed(1) + "%";

  const convEl = document.getElementById("shopConv");
  convEl.textContent = conv + "% open → buy";
  convEl.style.color = conv >= 5 ? "var(--success)" : conv >= 1 ? "var(--warning)" : "var(--text-dim)";

  renderShopChart("shopChart", data.rows || []);
  renderShopItems(data.items || []);
}

function renderShopItems(items) {
  const el = document.getElementById("shopItems");
  if (!items.length) {
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No purchases in range yet</div>';
    return;
  }
  const max = Math.max(1, ...items.map((i) => i.purchases || 0));
  let html = '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px">';
  for (const it of items) {
    const pct = ((it.purchases || 0) / max) * 100;
    const rev = it.currency === "robux"
      ? "R$ " + (it.revenue || 0).toLocaleString()
      : (it.revenue || 0).toLocaleString() + " 🪙";
    html += '<div style="position:relative;display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr auto auto;gap:12px;align-items:center;padding:8px 12px;background:var(--bg-input);border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;font-size:13px">'
      + '<div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;bottom:0;width:' + pct.toFixed(1) + '%;background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--accent-glow),transparent);border-left:2px solid var(--accent);border-radius:8px 0 0 8px;pointer-events:none"></div>'
      + '<div style="z-index:1;font-weight:600">' + escapeHtml(it.item_id) + ' <span style="color:var(--text-faint);font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:10px">' + escapeHtml(it.item_kind) + '</span></div>'
      + '<div style="z-index:1;font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">' + (it.purchases || 0) + '×</div>'
      + '<div style="z-index:1;font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:12px;color:var(--text)">' + rev + '</div>'
      + '</div>';
  }
  html += '</div>';
  el.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderShopChart(svgId, rows) {
  renderBarLineChart(svgId, rows, {
    emptyMsg: "no shop activity yet",
    padL: 40,
    lineOf: (r) => r.opens || 0,
    barOf: (r) => r.purchases || 0,
    barColor: "#5fc97a",
    barTitle: (r, buys) => r.date + ': ' + buys + ' purchases',
    lineColor: "#5bb0ff",
    lineTitle: (r, v) => r.date + ': ' + v + ' opens',
    legend: [
      { x: 600 - 150, color: "#5bb0ff", label: "opens" },
      { x: 600 - 95, color: "#5fc97a", label: "purchases" },
    ],
    entriesOf: (r) => [
      { name: "Opens", value: r.opens || 0, color: "#5bb0ff" },
      { name: "Purchases", value: r.purchases || 0, color: "#5fc97a" },
    ],
  });
}

async function loadClaims() {
  return safeLoad("loadClaims", "/stats/daily-claims?days=" + claimsDays, (data) => renderClaims(data));
}

function renderClaims(data) {
  const claims = data.claims || 0;
  const meta = document.getElementById("claimsMeta");
  meta.textContent = claims.toLocaleString() + " claims · " + (data.uniqueClaimers || 0).toLocaleString() + " players · " + (data.blockRate || 0) + "% set drops";
  meta.style.color = "var(--text-dim)";

  renderClaimsChart("claimsChart", data.rows || []);

  const el = document.getElementById("claimsSets");
  const sets = data.sets || [];
  if (!sets.length) {
    el.innerHTML = "";
    return;
  }
  const max = Math.max(1, ...sets.map((s) => s.drops || 0));
  let html = '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px">';
  for (const s of sets) {
    const pct = ((s.drops || 0) / max) * 100;
    html += '<div style="position:relative;display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr auto;gap:12px;align-items:center;padding:7px 12px;background:var(--bg-input);border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;font-size:13px">'
      + '<div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;bottom:0;width:' + pct.toFixed(1) + '%;background:linear-gradient(90deg,rgba(201,122,217,0.15),transparent);border-left:2px solid #c97ad9;border-radius:8px 0 0 8px;pointer-events:none"></div>'
      + '<div style="z-index:1;font-weight:600">' + escapeHtml(s.set_name) + '</div>'
      + '<div style="z-index:1;font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">' + (s.drops || 0) + ' drops</div>'
      + '</div>';
  }
  html += '</div>';
  el.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderClaimsChart(svgId, rows) {
  const svg = document.getElementById(svgId);
  svg.innerHTML = "";
  if (chartEmpty(svg, rows, "no claims yet")) return;
  const g = chartGeom(40);
  const max = Math.max(1, ...rows.map((r) => (r.coin_claims || 0) + (r.block_claims || 0)));
  const step = g.plotW / rows.length;
  const barW = Math.min(56, step * 0.8);
  svg.innerHTML += chartGrid(max, g, "");

  rows.forEach((r, i) => {
    const x = g.padL + i * step + (step - barW) / 2;
    const coin = r.coin_claims || 0;
    const block = r.block_claims || 0;
    const total = coin + block;
    const totalH = (total / max) * g.plotH;
    const coinH = (coin / max) * g.plotH;
    const blockH = totalH - coinH;

    if (blockH > 0) {
      svg.innerHTML += '<rect x="' + x + '" y="' + (g.padT + g.plotH - totalH) + '" width="' + barW + '" height="' + blockH + '" fill="#c97ad9" rx="1"><title>' + r.date + ': ' + block + ' set drops</title></rect>';
    }
    if (coinH > 0) {
      svg.innerHTML += '<rect x="' + x + '" y="' + (g.padT + g.plotH - coinH) + '" width="' + barW + '" height="' + coinH + '" fill="#5bb0ff" rx="1"><title>' + r.date + ': ' + coin + ' coin rolls</title></rect>';
    }
  });

  svg.innerHTML += chartXLabels(rows, g, (idx) => g.padL + idx * step + step / 2);
  svg.innerHTML += chartLegend([
    { x: 600 - 130, color: "#5bb0ff", label: "coins" },
    { x: 600 - 80, color: "#c97ad9", label: "set drops" },
  ]);

  const points = rows.map((r, i) => {
    const coin = r.coin_claims || 0;
    const block = r.block_claims || 0;
    return {
      x: g.padL + i * step + step / 2,
      markerY: g.padT + g.plotH - ((coin + block) / max) * g.plotH,
      markerColor: "#5bb0ff",
      label: r.date,
      entries: [
        { name: "Coin rolls", value: coin, color: "#5bb0ff" },
        { name: "Set drops", value: block, color: "#c97ad9" },
        { name: "Total", value: coin + block, color: null },
      ],
    };
  });
  attachChartTooltip(svgId, points);
}

async function loadOnboarding() {
  return safeLoad("loadOnboarding", "/stats/onboarding?days=" + onboardingDays, (data) => renderOnboarding(data));
}

function renderOnboarding(data) {
  const joined = data.joined || 0;
  const fb = data.firstBlock || 0;
  const fs = data.firstSave || 0;

  document.getElementById("onb-joined").textContent = joined.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("onb-block").textContent = fb.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("onb-save").textContent = fs.toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("onb-block-sub").textContent = (data.blockRate || 0) + "% of new";
  document.getElementById("onb-save-sub").textContent = (data.saveRate || 0) + "% of new";
  document.getElementById("onb-block-bar").style.width = (joined > 0 ? (fb / joined) * 100 : 0).toFixed(1) + "%";
  document.getElementById("onb-save-bar").style.width = (joined > 0 ? (fs / joined) * 100 : 0).toFixed(1) + "%";
}

async function loadSlots() {
  return safeLoad("loadSlots", "/stats/slots", (data) => renderSlots(data));
}

function renderSlots(data) {
  const meta = document.getElementById("slotsMeta");
  meta.textContent = (data.totalPlayers || 0).toLocaleString() + " savers · avg " + (data.avgSlots || 0) + " · " + (data.multiSlotRate || 0) + "% use 2+";
  meta.style.color = "var(--text-dim)";

  const content = document.getElementById("slotsContent");
  const rows = data.rows || [];
  if (!rows.length) {
    content.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No save data yet</div>';
    return;
  }
  const total = rows.reduce((a, r) => a + (r.players || 0), 0) || 1;
  const maxCount = Math.max(1, ...rows.map((r) => r.players || 0));

  let html = '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px">';
  for (const r of rows) {
    const players = r.players || 0;
    const barPct = (players / maxCount) * 100;
    const sharePct = Math.round((players / total) * 100);
    const label = r.slot_count + " save" + (r.slot_count === 1 ? "" : "s");
    html += '<div style="position:relative;display:grid;grid-template-columns:84px 1fr auto;gap:10px;align-items:center;padding:7px 12px;background:var(--bg-input);border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;font-size:13px">'
      + '<div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;bottom:0;width:' + barPct.toFixed(1) + '%;background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--accent-glow),transparent);border-left:2px solid var(--accent);border-radius:8px 0 0 8px;pointer-events:none"></div>'
      + '<div style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);z-index:1">' + label + '</div>'
      + '<div></div>'
      + '<div style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:12px;color:var(--text);z-index:1">' + players.toLocaleString() + ' <span style="color:var(--text-dim)">(' + sharePct + '%)</span></div>'
      + '</div>';
  }
  html += '</div>';
  content.innerHTML = html;
}

async function loadRetention() {
  return safeLoad("loadRetention", "/stats/retention?days=30", (data) => {
    renderRetention(data.rows || []);

    const rows = data.rows || [];
    let totalCohort = 0;
    let totalD1 = 0;
    for (const r of rows) {
      if (r.cohort_size > 0) {
        totalCohort += r.cohort_size;
        totalD1 += r.d1;
      }
    }
    const d1Pct = totalCohort > 0 ? Math.round((totalD1 / totalCohort) * 100) : 0;
    document.getElementById("kpi-d1").textContent = d1Pct + "%";
  });
}

function renderRetention(rows) {
  const content = document.getElementById("retentionContent");
  if (!rows.length) {
    content.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No cohort data yet</div>';
    return;
  }
  let html = '<table class="retention-table"><thead><tr><th>Cohort</th><th>Size</th><th>Day 1</th><th>Day 7</th><th>Day 30</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
  for (const r of rows.slice().reverse().slice(0, 14)) {
    const d1pct = r.cohort_size > 0 ? Math.round((r.d1 / r.cohort_size) * 100) : 0;
    const d7pct = r.cohort_size > 0 ? Math.round((r.d7 / r.cohort_size) * 100) : 0;
    const d30pct = r.cohort_size > 0 ? Math.round((r.d30 / r.cohort_size) * 100) : 0;
    html += '<tr>';
    html += '<td>' + escapeHtml(r.cohort_date) + '</td>';
    html += '<td>' + r.cohort_size + '</td>';
    html += '<td>' + r.d1 + ' <span class="pct">(' + d1pct + '%)</span></td>';
    html += '<td>' + r.d7 + ' <span class="pct">(' + d7pct + '%)</span></td>';
    html += '<td>' + r.d30 + ' <span class="pct">(' + d30pct + '%)</span></td>';
    html += '</tr>';
  }
  html += '</tbody></table>';
  content.innerHTML = html;
}

async function loadTopBlocks() {
  return safeLoad("loadTopBlocks", "/blocks/top?limit=10", (data) => renderTopBlocks(data));
}

function renderTopBlocks(data) {
  const content = document.getElementById("topBlocksContent");
  const ageBadge = document.getElementById("topBlocksAge");
  const rows = data.rows || [];

  if (rows.length && data.ageSeconds != null) {
    const a = data.ageSeconds;
    let label;
    if (a < 60) label = "updated " + a + "s ago";
    else if (a < 3600) label = "updated " + Math.floor(a / 60) + "m ago";
    else label = "updated " + Math.floor(a / 3600) + "h ago";
    ageBadge.textContent = label;
    ageBadge.style.display = "inline-flex";
  } else {
    ageBadge.style.display = "none";
  }

  if (!rows.length) {
    content.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No block data reported yet (Roblox posts top blocks every ~5 minutes)</div>';
    return;
  }

  const max = Math.max(1, ...rows.map((r) => r.count));
  let html = '<div class="topblocks">';
  rows.forEach((r, i) => {
    const pct = (r.count / max) * 100;
    html += '<div class="topblock-row">';
    html += '<div class="bar" style="width:' + pct.toFixed(1) + '%"></div>';
    html += '<div class="rank">#' + (i + 1) + '</div>';
    html += '<div class="name">' + escapeHtml(r.block_name) + '</div>';
    html += '<div class="count">' + r.count.toLocaleString() + '</div>';
    html += '</div>';
  });
  html += '</div>';
  content.innerHTML = html;
}

async function loadLeaderboards() {
  return safeLoad("loadLeaderboards", "/leaderboards", (data) => {
    renderLeaderboard("lbStreak", data.streak, (v) => "🔥 " + v);
    renderLeaderboard("lbLikes", data.likes, (v) => v.toLocaleString() + " ❤");
    renderLeaderboard("lbPlaytime", data.playtime, (v) => formatPlayTime(v));
    renderAllRounders(data);
  });
}

// Cross-board ranking: who shows up across the most leaderboards. Points per
// board reward a higher placement (top of a board of N = N points), so ties on
// board-count break by overall standing. Built entirely from the leaderboard
// payload already fetched — no extra request.
function renderAllRounders(data) {
  const boards = [
    { key: "streak", emoji: "🔥" },
    { key: "likes", emoji: "❤️" },
    { key: "playtime", emoji: "⏱️" },
  ];
  const players = {};
  for (const b of boards) {
    const list = data[b.key] || [];
    const n = list.length;
    for (const e of list) {
      const id = String(e.userId);
      if (!players[id]) players[id] = { username: e.username, boards: [], points: 0 };
      players[id].boards.push(b.emoji);
      players[id].points += (n - e.rank + 1);
    }
  }

  const ranked = Object.values(players).sort((a, b) =>
    (b.boards.length - a.boards.length) || (b.points - a.points)
  ).slice(0, 10);

  const el = document.getElementById("lbAllRounders");
  if (!ranked.length) {
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No data yet</div>';
    return;
  }
  let html = '<div class="lb-list">';
  ranked.forEach((p, i) => {
    html += '<div class="lb-row">';
    html += '<div class="lb-rank">#' + (i + 1) + '</div>';
    html += '<div class="lb-name">' + escapeHtml(p.username) + '</div>';
    html += '<div class="lb-value">' + p.boards.join("") + '</div>';
    html += '</div>';
  });
  html += '</div>';
  el.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderLeaderboard(elementId, entries, formatValue) {
  const el = document.getElementById(elementId);
  if (!entries || entries.length === 0) {
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No data yet</div>';
    return;
  }
  let html = '<div class="lb-list">';
  for (const e of entries) {
    html += '<div class="lb-row">';
    html += '<div class="lb-rank">#' + e.rank + '</div>';
    html += '<div class="lb-name">' + escapeHtml(e.username) + '</div>';
    html += '<div class="lb-value">' + formatValue(e.value) + '</div>';
    html += '</div>';
  }
  html += '</div>';
  el.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderStackedBarChart(svgId, rows) {
  const svg = document.getElementById(svgId);
  svg.innerHTML = "";
  if (!rows.length) {
    svg.innerHTML = '<text x="300" y="100" fill="#4a5170" text-anchor="middle" font-family="JetBrains Mono" font-size="12">no data</text>';
    return;
  }
  const W = 600, H = 200, padL = 40, padR = 12, padT = 12, padB = 30;
  const plotW = W - padL - padR;
  const plotH = H - padT - padB;
  const max = Math.max(1, ...rows.map((r) => (r.new_count || 0) + (r.returning_count || 0)));
  const barW = (plotW / rows.length) * 0.8;
  const step = plotW / rows.length;

  const yTicks = 4;
  for (let i = 0; i <= yTicks; i++) {
    const y = padT + plotH - (i / yTicks) * plotH;
    const v = Math.round((i / yTicks) * max);
    svg.innerHTML += '<line x1="' + padL + '" y1="' + y + '" x2="' + (W - padR) + '" y2="' + y + '" stroke="#1f2740" stroke-width="1"/>';
    svg.innerHTML += '<text x="' + (padL - 6) + '" y="' + (y + 3) + '" fill="#4a5170" text-anchor="end" font-family="JetBrains Mono" font-size="9">' + v + '</text>';
  }

  rows.forEach((r, i) => {
    const x = padL + i * step + (step - barW) / 2;
    const newCount = r.new_count || 0;
    const returningCount = r.returning_count || 0;
    const total = newCount + returningCount;
    const totalH = (total / max) * plotH;
    const newH = (newCount / max) * plotH;
    const retH = totalH - newH;

    if (retH > 0) {
      svg.innerHTML += '<rect x="' + x + '" y="' + (padT + plotH - retH) + '" width="' + barW + '" height="' + retH + '" fill="#5bb0ff" rx="1"><title>' + r.date + ': ' + returningCount + ' returning</title></rect>';
    }
    if (newH > 0) {
      svg.innerHTML += '<rect x="' + x + '" y="' + (padT + plotH - totalH) + '" width="' + barW + '" height="' + newH + '" fill="#5fc97a" rx="1"><title>' + r.date + ': ' + newCount + ' new</title></rect>';
    }
  });

  const labelCount = Math.min(6, rows.length);
  for (let i = 0; i < labelCount; i++) {
    const idx = Math.floor(i * (rows.length - 1) / Math.max(1, labelCount - 1));
    const x = padL + idx * step + step / 2;
    const label = (rows[idx].date || "").slice(5);
    svg.innerHTML += '<text x="' + x + '" y="' + (H - 10) + '" fill="#4a5170" text-anchor="middle" font-family="JetBrains Mono" font-size="9">' + label + '</text>';
  }
  svg.innerHTML += '<rect x="' + (W - 130) + '" y="4" width="8" height="8" fill="#5fc97a"/><text x="' + (W - 118) + '" y="11" fill="#7a83a0" font-family="JetBrains Mono" font-size="9">new</text>';
  svg.innerHTML += '<rect x="' + (W - 80) + '" y="4" width="8" height="8" fill="#5bb0ff"/><text x="' + (W - 68) + '" y="11" fill="#7a83a0" font-family="JetBrains Mono" font-size="9">returning</text>';

  const points = rows.map((r, i) => {
    const newC = r.new_count || 0;
    const retC = r.returning_count || 0;
    const total = newC + retC;
    return {
      x: padL + i * step + step / 2,
      markerY: padT + plotH - (total / max) * plotH,
      markerColor: "#5bb0ff",
      label: r.date,
      entries: [
        { name: "New", value: newC, color: "#5fc97a" },
        { name: "Returning", value: retC, color: "#5bb0ff" },
        { name: "Total", value: total, color: null },
      ],
    };
  });
  attachChartTooltip(svgId, points);
}

function renderLineChart(svgId, rows) {
  const svg = document.getElementById(svgId);
  svg.innerHTML = "";
  if (!rows.length) {
    svg.innerHTML = '<text x="300" y="100" fill="#4a5170" text-anchor="middle" font-family="JetBrains Mono" font-size="12">no data</text>';
    return;
  }
  const W = 600, H = 200, padL = 40, padR = 12, padT = 12, padB = 30;
  const plotW = W - padL - padR;
  const plotH = H - padT - padB;
  const max = Math.max(1, ...rows.map((r) => r.concurrent || 0));

  const yTicks = 4;
  for (let i = 0; i <= yTicks; i++) {
    const y = padT + plotH - (i / yTicks) * plotH;
    const v = Math.round((i / yTicks) * max);
    svg.innerHTML += '<line x1="' + padL + '" y1="' + y + '" x2="' + (W - padR) + '" y2="' + y + '" stroke="#1f2740" stroke-width="1"/>';
    svg.innerHTML += '<text x="' + (padL - 6) + '" y="' + (y + 3) + '" fill="#4a5170" text-anchor="end" font-family="JetBrains Mono" font-size="9">' + v + '</text>';
  }

  const pts = rows.map((r, i) => {
    const x = padL + (i / Math.max(1, rows.length - 1)) * plotW;
    const y = padT + plotH - ((r.concurrent || 0) / max) * plotH;
    return [x, y];
  });

  let fillPath = "M " + pts[0][0] + " " + (padT + plotH);
  pts.forEach((p) => { fillPath += " L " + p[0] + " " + p[1]; });
  fillPath += " L " + pts[pts.length - 1][0] + " " + (padT + plotH) + " Z";
  svg.innerHTML += '<path d="' + fillPath + '" fill="url(#concurrencyGrad)" opacity="0.3"/>';
  svg.innerHTML += '<defs><linearGradient id="concurrencyGrad" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1"><stop offset="0%" stop-color="#5bb0ff"/><stop offset="100%" stop-color="#5bb0ff" stop-opacity="0"/></linearGradient></defs>';

  let linePath = "M " + pts[0][0] + " " + pts[0][1];
  pts.forEach((p, i) => { if (i > 0) linePath += " L " + p[0] + " " + p[1]; });
  svg.innerHTML += '<path d="' + linePath + '" fill="none" stroke="#5bb0ff" stroke-width="2" stroke-linejoin="round"/>';

  const labelCount = Math.min(6, rows.length);
  for (let i = 0; i < labelCount; i++) {
    const idx = Math.floor(i * (rows.length - 1) / Math.max(1, labelCount - 1));
    const x = padL + (idx / Math.max(1, rows.length - 1)) * plotW;
    const label = (rows[idx].hour || "").slice(5, 13).replace("T", " ");
    svg.innerHTML += '<text x="' + x + '" y="' + (H - 10) + '" fill="#4a5170" text-anchor="middle" font-family="JetBrains Mono" font-size="9">' + label + '</text>';
  }

  const points = rows.map((r, i) => ({
    x: pts[i][0],
    markerY: pts[i][1],
    markerColor: "#5bb0ff",
    label: ((r.hour || "").slice(0, 16).replace("T", " ")) + " UTC",
    entries: [{ name: "Concurrent", value: r.concurrent || 0, color: "#5bb0ff" }],
  }));
  attachChartTooltip(svgId, points);
}

// ---- Chart tap/click tooltips ---------------------------------------------
// SVGs use preserveAspectRatio="none", so we map the tap's client coords back to
// chart user-space via getScreenCTM().inverse(), find the nearest point by x, then
// draw an SVG guide line + marker and position a crisp HTML tooltip over the card.

function clearAllChartTooltips() {
  document.querySelectorAll(".chart-card").forEach((card) => {
    const tip = card.querySelector(".chart-tooltip");
    if (tip) tip.remove();
    const svg = card.querySelector("svg");
    if (svg) { const hl = svg.querySelector(".chart-hl"); if (hl) hl.remove(); }
  });
}

function hideChartTooltip(svg, card) {
  const hl = svg.querySelector(".chart-hl");
  if (hl) hl.remove();
  const tip = card.querySelector(".chart-tooltip");
  if (tip) tip.remove();
}

function attachChartTooltip(svgId, points) {
  const svg = document.getElementById(svgId);
  if (!svg) return;
  const card = svg.closest(".chart-card");
  if (!card) return;
  svg._ttPoints = points;
  hideChartTooltip(svg, card);
  if (svg._ttBound) return;
  svg._ttBound = true;
  svg.addEventListener("click", (e) => {
    const pts = svg._ttPoints || [];
    if (!pts.length) return;
    const ctm = svg.getScreenCTM();
    if (!ctm) return;
    const sp = svg.createSVGPoint();
    sp.x = e.clientX;
    sp.y = e.clientY;
    const userX = sp.matrixTransform(ctm.inverse()).x;
    let nearest = 0, best = Infinity;
    for (let i = 0; i < pts.length; i++) {
      const d = Math.abs(pts[i].x - userX);
      if (d < best) { best = d; nearest = i; }
    }
    showChartTooltip(svg, card, pts[nearest]);
  });
}

function showChartTooltip(svg, card, p) {
  clearAllChartTooltips();
  const NS = "http://www.w3.org/2000/svg";
  const color = p.markerColor || "#5bb0ff";

  const g = document.createElementNS(NS, "g");
  g.setAttribute("class", "chart-hl");
  g.setAttribute("pointer-events", "none");

  const line = document.createElementNS(NS, "line");
  line.setAttribute("x1", p.x); line.setAttribute("x2", p.x);
  line.setAttribute("y1", "12"); line.setAttribute("y2", "170");
  line.setAttribute("stroke", color);
  line.setAttribute("stroke-width", "1");
  line.setAttribute("stroke-dasharray", "3 3");
  line.setAttribute("opacity", "0.55");
  g.appendChild(line);

  if (p.markerY != null) {
    const dot = document.createElementNS(NS, "circle");
    dot.setAttribute("cx", p.x); dot.setAttribute("cy", p.markerY);
    dot.setAttribute("r", "4");
    dot.setAttribute("fill", "#0d111c");
    dot.setAttribute("stroke", color);
    dot.setAttribute("stroke-width", "2");
    g.appendChild(dot);
  }
  svg.appendChild(g);

  const tip = document.createElement("div");
  tip.className = "chart-tooltip";
  let html = '<div class="tt-date">' + escapeHtml(p.label) + '</div>';
  for (const ent of p.entries) {
    html += '<div class="tt-row">';
    html += '<span class="tt-dot" style="background:' + (ent.color || "transparent") + '"></span>';
    html += '<span class="tt-name">' + escapeHtml(ent.name) + '</span>';
    html += '<span class="tt-val">' + escapeHtml(String(ent.value)) + '</span>';
    html += '</div>';
  }
  tip.innerHTML = html;
  card.appendChild(tip);

  const sp = svg.createSVGPoint();
  sp.x = p.x;
  sp.y = p.markerY != null ? p.markerY : 40;
  const screen = sp.matrixTransform(svg.getScreenCTM());
  const cardRect = card.getBoundingClientRect();
  const left = screen.x - cardRect.left;
  const top = screen.y - cardRect.top;
  tip.style.left = left + "px";
  tip.style.top = top + "px";

  requestAnimationFrame(() => {
    const tw = tip.offsetWidth;
    const th = tip.offsetHeight;
    const cw = card.clientWidth;
    let l = left;
    if (l - tw / 2 < 4) l = tw / 2 + 4;
    if (l + tw / 2 > cw - 4) l = cw - 4 - tw / 2;
    tip.style.left = l + "px";
    // Flip below the point if there isn't room above it.
    tip.style.transform = (top - th - 12 < 0)
      ? "translate(-50%, 14px)"
      : "translate(-50%, calc(-100% - 12px))";
    tip.style.opacity = "1";
  });
}

// Tap anywhere that isn't a chart to dismiss any open tooltip.
document.addEventListener("click", (e) => {
  if (e.target.closest && e.target.closest(".chart-card svg")) return;
  clearAllChartTooltips();
});

// ===========================================================================
// Players + Economy tabs
// ===========================================================================
let acquisitionDays = 30;
let heatmapDays = 30;
let sessionSplitDays = 30;
let coinflowDays = 30;
let shopDetailDays = 30;
let plusQualityDays = 30;

// Horizontal labelled bars — the shared pattern used by every distribution and
// ranking panel below. opt: { valueKey, labelKey, label(it), fmt(v,it), color, empty }.
function renderHBars(containerId, items, opt) {
  const el = document.getElementById(containerId);
  if (!el) return;
  if (!items || !items.length) {
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">' + (opt.empty || "No data yet") + '</div>';
    return;
  }
  const color = opt.color || "#5bb0ff";
  const max = Math.max(1, ...items.map((it) => it[opt.valueKey] || 0));
  let html = '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px">';
  for (const it of items) {
    const v = it[opt.valueKey] || 0;
    const pct = (v / max) * 100;
    const label = opt.label ? opt.label(it) : escapeHtml(String(it[opt.labelKey]));
    const valTxt = opt.fmt ? opt.fmt(v, it) : v.toLocaleString();
    html += '<div style="position:relative;display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr auto;gap:12px;align-items:center;padding:7px 12px;background:var(--bg-input);border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;font-size:13px">'
      + '<div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;bottom:0;width:' + pct.toFixed(1) + '%;background:linear-gradient(90deg,' + color + '22,transparent);border-left:2px solid ' + color + ';border-radius:8px 0 0 8px;pointer-events:none"></div>'
      + '<div style="z-index:1;font-weight:600">' + label + '</div>'
      + '<div style="z-index:1;font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">' + valTxt + '</div>'
      + '</div>';
  }
  html += '</div>';
  el.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderPlayerbase(data) {
  const c = data.churn || {};
  const lt = data.lifetime || {};
  document.getElementById("pb-total").textContent = (lt.total || 0).toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("pb-active7").textContent = (c.active7 || 0).toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("pb-active7-sub").textContent = (c.active1 || 0).toLocaleString() + " in last 24h";
  document.getElementById("pb-lapsed").textContent = (c.lapsed_30p || 0).toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("pb-react-sub").textContent = (c.reactivated7 || 0).toLocaleString() + " returned this week";
  document.getElementById("pb-lifetime").textContent = (lt.avgDays || 0) + "d";
  document.getElementById("pb-sessions-sub").textContent = (lt.avgSessions || 0) + " sessions avg";
  document.getElementById("pb-active14").textContent = (c.active14 || 0).toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("pb-active30").textContent = (c.active30 || 0).toLocaleString();

  renderMultiLineChart("acquisitionChart", data.acquisition || [], {
    emptyMsg: "no joins yet",
    padL: 40,
    maxOf: (r) => r.count || 0,
    series: [{ key: "count", color: "#5fc97a" }],
    legend: [{ x: 600 - 120, color: "#5fc97a", label: "new players" }],
    markerColor: "#5fc97a",
    markerOf: (r) => r.count || 0,
    entriesOf: (r) => [{ name: "New players", value: r.count || 0, color: "#5fc97a" }],
  });

  renderHBars("churnLapsed", [
    { label: "Lapsed 7–14d", v: c.lapsed_7_14 || 0 },
    { label: "Lapsed 14–30d", v: c.lapsed_14_30 || 0 },
    { label: "Lapsed 30d+", v: c.lapsed_30p || 0 },
  ], { valueKey: "v", labelKey: "label", color: "#ffc266", empty: "No lapsed players" });

  const order = ["1", "2-4", "5-9", "10-24", "25+"];
  const sb = (data.sessionBuckets || []).slice().sort((a, b) => order.indexOf(a.bucket) - order.indexOf(b.bucket));
  renderHBars("sessionBuckets", sb, {
    valueKey: "count",
    label: (it) => escapeHtml(it.bucket) + " session" + (it.bucket === "1" ? "" : "s"),
    color: "#5bb0ff",
    empty: "No sessions yet",
  });
}

function renderHeatmap(data) {
  const cells = data.cells || [];
  const el = document.getElementById("heatmapContent");
  const metaEl = document.getElementById("heatmapMeta");
  if (!cells.length) {
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No sessions yet</div>';
    metaEl.textContent = "";
    return;
  }
  const grid = {};
  let max = 0, total = 0, best = null;
  for (const c of cells) {
    grid[c.dow + "_" + c.hour] = c.count;
    if (c.count > max) max = c.count;
    total += c.count;
    if (!best || c.count > best.count) best = c;
  }
  const days = ["Sun", "Mon", "Tue", "Wed", "Thu", "Fri", "Sat"];
  let html = '<div style="overflow-x:auto"><div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:34px repeat(24,1fr);gap:2px;min-width:560px;font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:9px">';
  html += '<div></div>';
  for (let h = 0; h < 24; h++) html += '<div style="text-align:center;color:var(--text-dim)">' + (h % 6 === 0 ? h : "") + '</div>';
  for (let d = 0; d < 7; d++) {
    html += '<div style="color:var(--text-dim);display:flex;align-items:center">' + days[d] + '</div>';
    for (let h = 0; h < 24; h++) {
      const v = grid[d + "_" + h] || 0;
      const a = max ? (0.12 + 0.88 * (v / max)) : 0;
      const bg = v ? 'rgba(91,176,255,' + a.toFixed(3) + ')' : 'var(--bg-input)';
      html += '<div title="' + days[d] + ' ' + h + ':00 — ' + v + ' sessions" style="height:16px;border-radius:3px;background:' + bg + '"></div>';
    }
  }
  html += '</div></div>';
  el.innerHTML = html;
  const bd = best ? (days[best.dow] + " " + best.hour + ":00") : "—";
  metaEl.textContent = "busiest: " + bd + " · " + total.toLocaleString() + " sessions";
}

function renderSessionSplit(data) {
  renderMultiLineChart("sessionSplitChart", data.rows || [], {
    emptyMsg: "no completed sessions yet",
    padL: 40,
    maxOf: (r) => Math.max(r.new_avg || 0, r.ret_avg || 0),
    series: [{ key: "new_avg", color: "#5fc97a" }, { key: "ret_avg", color: "#5bb0ff" }],
    legend: [{ x: 600 - 150, color: "#5fc97a", label: "new" }, { x: 600 - 95, color: "#5bb0ff", label: "returning" }],
    markerColor: "#5bb0ff",
    markerOf: (r) => Math.max(r.new_avg || 0, r.ret_avg || 0),
    entriesOf: (r) => [
      { name: "New", value: Math.round(r.new_avg || 0) + "m", color: "#5fc97a" },
      { name: "Returning", value: Math.round(r.ret_avg || 0) + "m", color: "#5bb0ff" },
    ],
  });
  const order = ["<1m", "1-5m", "5-10m", "10-30m", "30-60m", "60m+"];
  const h = (data.histogram || []).slice().sort((a, b) => order.indexOf(a.bucket) - order.indexOf(b.bucket));
  renderHBars("sessionHist", h, { valueKey: "count", labelKey: "bucket", color: "#c97ad9", empty: "No completed sessions" });
}

function renderMilestones(data) {
  const joined = data.joined || 0;
  renderHBars("milestonesContent", data.rows || [], {
    valueKey: "users",
    labelKey: "milestone",
    color: "#5fc97a",
    fmt: (v) => v.toLocaleString() + (joined > 0 ? " (" + Math.round((v / joined) * 100) + "%)" : ""),
    empty: "No milestones recorded",
  });
}

function renderServers(data) {
  const el = document.getElementById("serversContent");
  const servers = data.servers || [];
  if (!servers.length) {
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No live servers</div>';
    return;
  }
  const max = Math.max(1, ...servers.map((s) => s.players || 0));
  let html = '<div style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-bottom:8px">'
    + data.serverCount + ' servers · ' + (data.totalPlayers || 0) + ' players · avg ' + (data.avgPlayers || 0) + '/server</div>';
  html += '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px">';
  for (const s of servers.slice(0, 12)) {
    const pct = ((s.players || 0) / max) * 100;
    const up = formatPlayTime(s.uptimeSeconds || 0);
    html += '<div style="position:relative;display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr auto;gap:12px;align-items:center;padding:7px 12px;background:var(--bg-input);border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;font-size:13px">'
      + '<div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;bottom:0;width:' + pct.toFixed(1) + '%;background:linear-gradient(90deg,#5bb0ff22,transparent);border-left:2px solid #5bb0ff;border-radius:8px 0 0 8px;pointer-events:none"></div>'
      + '<div style="z-index:1;font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:11px">' + escapeHtml(String(s.serverId).slice(0, 8)) + ' · up ' + up + '</div>'
      + '<div style="z-index:1;font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">' + (s.players || 0) + ' players</div>'
      + '</div>';
  }
  html += '</div>';
  el.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderCoinflow(data) {
  const rows = (data.rows || []).slice();
  let bal = 0;
  for (const r of rows) {
    bal += (r.earned || 0) - (r.spent || 0);
    r.cumulative = bal;
  }
  renderMultiLineChart("coinflowChart", rows, {
    emptyMsg: "no coin activity yet",
    padL: 52,
    maxOf: (r) => Math.max(0, r.cumulative || 0),
    series: [{ key: "cumulative", color: "#5fc97a" }],
    legend: [{ x: 600 - 150, color: "#5fc97a", label: "net coin balance" }],
    markerColor: "#5fc97a",
    markerOf: (r) => Math.max(0, r.cumulative || 0),
    entriesOf: (r) => [
      { name: "Balance", value: (r.cumulative || 0).toLocaleString(), color: "#5fc97a" },
      { name: "Earned", value: (r.earned || 0).toLocaleString(), color: null },
      { name: "Spent", value: (r.spent || 0).toLocaleString(), color: null },
    ],
  });
  const meta = document.getElementById("coinflowMeta");
  const sign = bal >= 0 ? "+" : "";
  meta.textContent = sign + bal.toLocaleString() + " net over period";
  meta.style.color = bal > 0 ? "var(--warning)" : "var(--success)";

  const whales = (data.whales || []).map((w, i) => ({ rank: i + 1, username: w.username, user_id: w.user_id, spent: w.spent }));
  renderHBars("coinWhales", whales, {
    valueKey: "spent",
    label: (it) => "#" + it.rank + " " + escapeHtml(it.username || String(it.user_id)),
    fmt: (v) => v.toLocaleString() + " spent",
    color: "#ffc266",
    empty: "No spending yet",
  });

  document.getElementById("ec-spender").textContent = (data.spenderRate || 0) + "%";
  document.getElementById("ec-avgspend").textContent = (data.avgSpendPerSpender || 0).toLocaleString();
}

function renderShopDetail(data) {
  renderHBars("shopCurrency", data.byCurrency || [], {
    valueKey: "purchases",
    labelKey: "currency",
    color: "#5bb0ff",
    fmt: (v, it) => v.toLocaleString() + " buys · " + (it.revenue || 0).toLocaleString(),
    empty: "No purchases",
  });
  renderHBars("shopKind", data.byKind || [], {
    valueKey: "purchases",
    labelKey: "kind",
    color: "#c97ad9",
    fmt: (v, it) => v.toLocaleString() + " buys · " + (it.revenue || 0).toLocaleString(),
    empty: "No purchases",
  });
  document.getElementById("shopDetailMeta").textContent =
    (data.buyers || 0).toLocaleString() + " buyers · " + (data.repeatRate || 0) + "% repeat";
  document.getElementById("ec-repeat").textContent = (data.repeatRate || 0) + "%";
  document.getElementById("ec-ttf-sub").textContent = (data.avgDaysToFirstPurchase || 0) + " days to 1st buy";
}

function renderStreaks(data) {
  const order = ["1", "2-3", "4-6", "7-13", "14-29", "30+"];
  const b = (data.buckets || []).slice().sort((a, b) => order.indexOf(a.bucket) - order.indexOf(b.bucket));
  renderHBars("streakBuckets", b, {
    valueKey: "count",
    label: (it) => escapeHtml(it.bucket) + " day" + (it.bucket === "1" ? "" : "s"),
    color: "#ffc266",
    empty: "No claims yet",
  });
  renderHBars("streakSets", data.sets || [], {
    valueKey: "drops",
    labelKey: "set_name",
    color: "#c97ad9",
    fmt: (v, it) => v.toLocaleString() + " drops · " + (it.players || 0) + " players",
    empty: "No set drops yet",
  });
}

function renderPlusQuality(data) {
  document.getElementById("ec-wasted").textContent = (data.wastedRate || 0) + "%";
  const meta = document.getElementById("plusQualityMeta");
  meta.textContent = (data.taps || 0).toLocaleString() + " taps · " + (data.wasted || 0).toLocaleString() + " wasted · " + (data.purchases || 0) + " bought";
  meta.style.color = "var(--text-dim)";
  renderHBars("plusQualitySources", data.sources || [], {
    valueKey: "taps",
    labelKey: "source",
    color: "#5bb0ff",
    fmt: (v, it) => v.toLocaleString() + " taps · " + (it.wasted || 0) + " wasted · " + (it.purchases || 0) + " bought",
    empty: "No Plus taps yet",
  });
}

// ===========================================================================
// History trend panels (block popularity, engagement, saves-per-player)
// ===========================================================================
let blockTrendsDays = 30;
let engagementDays = 30;
let slotsTrendDays = 30;

async function loadBlockTrends() {
  return safeLoad("loadBlockTrends", "/stats/block-trends?days=" + blockTrendsDays, (d) => renderBlockTrends(d));
}
async function loadEngagementTrends() {
  return safeLoad("loadEngagementTrends", "/stats/engagement-trends?days=" + engagementDays, (d) => renderEngagementTrends(d));
}
async function loadSlotsTrends() {
  return safeLoad("loadSlotsTrends", "/stats/slots-trends?days=" + slotsTrendDays, (d) => renderSlotsTrends(d));
}

function renderBlockTrends(data) {
  const palette = ["#5bb0ff", "#5fc97a", "#c97ad9", "#ffc266", "#ff7a7a", "#7ad9d9"];
  const blocks = data.blocks || [];
  const dates = data.dates || [];
  const rows = dates.map((d, i) => {
    const o = { date: d };
    blocks.forEach((b, bi) => { o["b" + bi] = b.counts[i] || 0; });
    return o;
  });
  const series = blocks.map((b, bi) => ({ key: "b" + bi, color: palette[bi % palette.length] }));
  renderMultiLineChart("blockTrendsChart", rows, {
    emptyMsg: "no block history yet",
    padL: 44,
    maxOf: (r) => Math.max(0, ...series.map((s) => r[s.key] || 0)),
    series: series.length ? series : [{ key: "b0", color: palette[0] }],
    legend: [],
    markerColor: palette[0],
    markerOf: (r) => Math.max(0, ...series.map((s) => r[s.key] || 0)),
    entriesOf: (r) => blocks.map((b, bi) => ({ name: b.name, value: r["b" + bi] || 0, color: palette[bi % palette.length] })),
  });
  const el = document.getElementById("blockTrendsMovers");
  if (!blocks.length) {
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No block history yet — it starts filling once you create the block_history table</div>';
    return;
  }
  let html = '<div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:6px">';
  blocks.forEach((b, bi) => {
    const d = b.delta || 0;
    const arrow = d > 0 ? "▲" : (d < 0 ? "▼" : "·");
    const col = d > 0 ? "var(--success)" : (d < 0 ? "#ff7a7a" : "var(--text-dim)");
    html += '<span class="pill" style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;font-family:var(--font-mono)">'
      + '<span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:2px;background:' + palette[bi % palette.length] + '"></span>'
      + escapeHtml(b.name) + ' ' + (b.last || 0).toLocaleString()
      + ' <span style="color:' + col + '">' + arrow + ' ' + Math.abs(d).toLocaleString() + '</span></span>';
  });
  html += '</div>';
  el.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderEngagementTrends(data) {
  const rows = data.rows || [];
  renderAreaChart("engagementChart", rows, {
    emptyMsg: "no engagement snapshots yet",
    padL: 52,
    suffix: "",
    color: "#ffc266",
    gradId: "engGrad",
    valueOf: (r) => Math.round(r.avg_coins || 0),
    titleOf: (r, v) => r.date + ': ' + v.toLocaleString() + ' avg coins',
    entriesOf: (r, v) => [
      { name: "Avg coins", value: v.toLocaleString(), color: "#ffc266" },
      { name: "Avg streak", value: Math.round(r.avg_streak || 0), color: null },
      { name: "Avg likes", value: Math.round(r.avg_likes || 0), color: null },
      { name: "Players", value: r.players || 0, color: null },
    ],
  });
  const meta = document.getElementById("engagementMeta");
  const last = rows.length ? rows[rows.length - 1] : null;
  meta.textContent = last
    ? ("latest: " + Math.round(last.avg_coins || 0).toLocaleString() + " coins · " + Math.round(last.avg_streak || 0) + " streak · " + Math.round(last.avg_likes || 0) + " likes")
    : "";
}

function renderSlotsTrends(data) {
  const rows = data.rows || [];
  renderAreaChart("slotsTrendChart", rows, {
    emptyMsg: "no save snapshots yet",
    padL: 40,
    suffix: "",
    color: "#5fc97a",
    gradId: "slotsTrendGrad",
    valueOf: (r) => r.avg_slots || 0,
    titleOf: (r, v) => r.date + ': ' + (Math.round(v * 100) / 100) + ' avg saves',
    entriesOf: (r, v) => [
      { name: "Avg saves", value: Math.round((r.avg_slots || 0) * 100) / 100, color: "#5fc97a" },
      { name: "Multi-save %", value: (r.multi_slot_rate || 0) + "%", color: null },
      { name: "Savers", value: r.total_players || 0, color: null },
    ],
  });
  const meta = document.getElementById("slotsTrendMeta");
  const last = rows.length ? rows[rows.length - 1] : null;
  meta.textContent = last ? ((last.multi_slot_rate || 0) + "% use 2+ saves") : "";
}

setupRangeButtons("#blockTrendsRange", (v) => { blockTrendsDays = v; }, loadBlockTrends);
setupRangeButtons("#engagementRange", (v) => { engagementDays = v; }, loadEngagementTrends);
setupRangeButtons("#slotsTrendRange", (v) => { slotsTrendDays = v; }, loadSlotsTrends);

// ===========================================================================
// Chat tab
// ===========================================================================
let chatDays = 30;
let chatFilter = "all";
let chatQuery = "";
let chatSearchTimer = null;

const CHAT_CAT_COLORS = {
  complaint: "#ff7a7a", bug: "#ffc266", toxic: "#ff5d5d", praise: "#5fc97a",
  suggestion: "#5bb0ff", question: "#7ad9d9", social: "#c97ad9",
  chatter: "#7a83a0", other: "#7a83a0",
};
function chatCatColor(c) { return CHAT_CAT_COLORS[c] || "#7a83a0"; }

async function apiPost(path) {
  const token = tokenInput.value.trim();
  if (!token) throw new Error("No admin token set");
  const target = targetSelect.value;
  const sep = path.includes("?") ? "&" : "?";
  const res = await fetch(path + sep + "target=" + encodeURIComponent(target), {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "X-Admin-Token": token },
  });
  if (!res.ok) { const t = await res.text(); throw new Error("HTTP " + res.status + " — " + t); }
  return res.json();
}

async function loadChat() {
  let path = "/stats/chat?days=" + chatDays;
  if (chatFilter === "complaints") path += "&complaints=1";
  else if (chatFilter !== "all") path += "&category=" + encodeURIComponent(chatFilter);
  if (chatQuery) path += "&q=" + encodeURIComponent(chatQuery);
  return safeLoad("loadChat", path, (d) => renderChat(d));
}

function renderChat(data) {
  const tot = data.totals || {};
  document.getElementById("chat-total").textContent = (tot.total || 0).toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("chat-complaints").textContent = (tot.complaints || 0).toLocaleString();
  document.getElementById("chat-complaints-sub").textContent =
    (tot.total > 0 ? Math.round((tot.complaints / tot.total) * 100) : 0) + "% of messages";
  document.getElementById("chat-unclassified").textContent = (tot.unclassified || 0).toLocaleString();

  renderMultiLineChart("chatChart", data.rows || [], {
    emptyMsg: "no chat captured yet",
    padL: 40,
    maxOf: (r) => r.total || 0,
    series: [{ key: "total", color: "#5bb0ff" }, { key: "complaints", color: "#ff7a7a" }],
    legend: [{ x: 600 - 165, color: "#5bb0ff", label: "messages" }, { x: 600 - 95, color: "#ff7a7a", label: "complaints" }],
    markerColor: "#5bb0ff",
    markerOf: (r) => r.total || 0,
    entriesOf: (r) => [
      { name: "Messages", value: r.total || 0, color: "#5bb0ff" },
      { name: "Complaints", value: r.complaints || 0, color: "#ff7a7a" },
    ],
  });

  renderHBars("chatCategories", data.categories || [], {
    valueKey: "count",
    color: "#5bb0ff",
    label: (it) => '<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:6px">'
      + '<span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:2px;background:' + chatCatColor(it.category) + '"></span>'
      + escapeHtml(it.category || "?") + '</span>',
    empty: "No messages yet",
  });

  const el = document.getElementById("chatFeed");
  const feed = data.feed || [];
  if (!feed.length) {
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No messages match</div>';
  } else {
    let html = "";
    for (const m of feed) {
      const col = chatCatColor(m.category);
      const border = m.is_complaint ? "1px solid rgba(255,93,93,0.55)" : "1px solid rgba(127,131,160,0.18)";
      html += '<div style="border:' + border + ';border-radius:8px;padding:8px 10px;margin-bottom:6px;background:var(--bg-input)">'
        + '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;align-items:center;margin-bottom:3px;font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim)">'
        + '<span style="font-weight:700;color:var(--text)">' + escapeHtml(m.username || "?") + '</span>'
        + '<span class="pill" style="background:' + col + '22;color:' + col + '">' + escapeHtml(m.category || "?") + '</span>'
        + (m.sentiment ? '<span>' + escapeHtml(m.sentiment) + '</span>' : '')
        + '<span style="margin-left:auto">' + escapeHtml(fbDate(m.created_at)) + '</span></div>'
        + '<div style="font-size:13px;word-break:break-word">' + escapeHtml(m.message || "") + '</div>'
        + '</div>';
    }
    el.innerHTML = html;
  }

  document.getElementById("chatMeta").textContent =
    (tot.total || 0).toLocaleString() + " messages · " + (tot.unclassified || 0) + " to classify";
}

async function classifyChat() {
  const btn = document.getElementById("chatClassifyBtn");
  const st = document.getElementById("chatClassifyStatus");
  btn.disabled = true;
  st.textContent = "classifying…";
  try {
    const r = await apiPost("/chat/classify");
    st.textContent = r.error ? r.error : ("classified " + (r.classified || 0) + " · " + (r.remaining || 0) + " left");
    loadChat();
  } catch (e) {
    st.textContent = "failed: " + e.message;
  }
  btn.disabled = false;
}

function loadChatTab() { loadChat(); }

setupRangeButtons("#chatRange", (v) => { chatDays = v; }, loadChat);
document.querySelectorAll("#chatFilter button").forEach((b) => {
  b.addEventListener("click", () => {
    document.querySelectorAll("#chatFilter button").forEach((x) => x.classList.remove("active"));
    b.classList.add("active");
    chatFilter = b.dataset.filter;
    loadChat();
  });
});
document.getElementById("chatSearch").addEventListener("input", (e) => {
  clearTimeout(chatSearchTimer);
  chatQuery = e.target.value.trim();
  chatSearchTimer = setTimeout(loadChat, 350);
});
document.getElementById("chatClassifyBtn").addEventListener("click", classifyChat);

function escapeHtml(s) {
  return String(s).replace(/[&<>"']/g, (c) => ({
    "&": "&amp;",
    "<": "&lt;",
    ">": "&gt;",
    '"': "&quot;",
    "'": "&#39;",
  }[c]));
}

// ===========================================================================
// Gifts tab
// ===========================================================================
// REWARD_SETS is the single source of truth for what the admin panel offers.
// When you ship a new RewardSet folder under ReplicatedStorage.RewardSets in
// Roblox, ADD AN ENTRY HERE so it shows up in the gift picker. The "name"
// MUST match the folder name in Roblox exactly (case-sensitive on the server).
const REWARD_SETS = [
  { name: "RainbowBlocks", rarity: "Rare", description: "Color-cycling rainbow blocks (4 blocks)" },
  { name: "CandyBlocks", rarity: "Rare", description: "Candy bricks, chocolate, candy canes, candy lattice + sapling" },
];
let resolvedGiftUser = null;
let giftsInitialized = false;
function rarityPillClass(r) {
  const v = String(r || "").toLowerCase();
  if (v === "rare") return "warning";
  if (v === "uncommon") return "info";
  return "new"; // common
}
function buildSetsList(containerId) {
  const el = document.getElementById(containerId);
  if (!el) return;
  el.innerHTML = "";
  if (REWARD_SETS.length === 0) {
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state" style="padding:14px">No reward sets configured. Edit REWARD_SETS in the Worker.</div>';
    return;
  }
  REWARD_SETS.forEach((s) => {
    const label = document.createElement("label");
    label.className = "set-chip";
    label.innerHTML =
      '<input type="checkbox" value="' + escapeHtml(s.name) + '">' +
      '<div class="chip-content">' +
        '<div class="chip-name">' + escapeHtml(s.name) + ' <span class="pill ' + rarityPillClass(s.rarity) + '">' + escapeHtml(s.rarity || "Common") + '</span></div>' +
        '<div class="chip-desc">' + escapeHtml(s.description || "") + '</div>' +
      '</div>';
    el.appendChild(label);
  });
  el.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(cb => {
    cb.addEventListener("change", () => {
      cb.closest(".set-chip").classList.toggle("selected", cb.checked);
      if (containerId === "gift-sets-list") refreshGiftSendState();
      else refreshGiftAllSendState();
    });
  });
}
function getSelectedSets(containerId) {
  const el = document.getElementById(containerId);
  if (!el) return [];
  return Array.from(el.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]:checked')).map(cb => cb.value);
}
function refreshGiftSendState() {
  const btn = document.getElementById("gift-send-btn");
  const sets = getSelectedSets("gift-sets-list");
  btn.disabled = !resolvedGiftUser || sets.length === 0;
}
function refreshGiftAllSendState() {
  const btn = document.getElementById("gift-send-all-btn");
  const sets = getSelectedSets("gift-all-sets-list");
  btn.disabled = sets.length === 0;
}
function initGifts() {
  if (!giftsInitialized) {
    buildSetsList("gift-sets-list");
    buildSetsList("gift-all-sets-list");
    giftsInitialized = true;
  }
  refreshGiftLive();
  startGiftPolling();
}
// ---- Gift live data (shared by online-count + player picker) ------------
// One /stats/live fetch updates BOTH the "X online" count card and the picker
// list, so polling doesn't double up. Polling auto-starts when the Gifts tab
// is opened and stops when leaving the tab (see activateTab + stopGiftPolling).
const GIFT_REFRESH_INTERVAL_MS = 15000;
let giftPollTimer = null;
let giftLiveData = null;
let giftLiveFetchedAt = 0;
let giftPickerSelectedUserId = null;
function startGiftPolling() {
  if (giftPollTimer) return;
  giftPollTimer = setInterval(refreshGiftLive, GIFT_REFRESH_INTERVAL_MS);
}
function stopGiftPolling() {
  if (giftPollTimer) { clearInterval(giftPollTimer); giftPollTimer = null; }
}
async function refreshGiftLive() {
  if (!tokenInput.value.trim()) {
    renderGiftOnlineCount(null, "Set admin token to load count");
    renderGiftPickerList(null, "Set admin token");
    return;
  }
  try {
    const data = await apiGet("/stats/live");
    giftLiveData = data;
    giftLiveFetchedAt = Date.now();
    renderGiftOnlineCount(data, null);
    renderGiftPickerList(data, null);
  } catch (err) {
    renderGiftOnlineCount(null, "Live data unavailable: " + err.message);
    renderGiftPickerList(null, "Live data unavailable: " + err.message);
  }
}
function renderGiftOnlineCount(data, errMsg) {
  const el = document.getElementById("gift-online-count");
  if (!el) return;
  const textEl = el.querySelector(".online-text");
  if (errMsg) {
    el.classList.add("empty");
    textEl.textContent = errMsg;
    return;
  }
  const players = data.playerCount || 0;
  const servers = data.serverCount || 0;
  el.classList.toggle("empty", players === 0);
  textEl.textContent = players + " player" + (players === 1 ? "" : "s") + " on " + servers + " server" + (servers === 1 ? "" : "s") + " (" + targetSelect.value.toUpperCase() + ")";
}
function renderGiftPickerList(data, errMsg) {
  const metaText = document.getElementById("gift-picker-meta-text");
  const metaEl = document.getElementById("gift-picker-meta");
  const listEl = document.getElementById("gift-picker-list");
  if (!listEl || !metaText) return;
  if (errMsg) {
    metaEl.classList.add("stale");
    metaText.textContent = errMsg;
    listEl.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">' + escapeHtml(errMsg) + '</div>';
    return;
  }
  metaEl.classList.remove("stale");
  const players = data.players || [];
  metaText.textContent = players.length + " online · " + (data.serverCount || 0) + " server" + (data.serverCount === 1 ? "" : "s") + " · " + targetSelect.value.toUpperCase();
  if (players.length === 0) {
    listEl.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No players online right now</div>';
    return;
  }
  const query = (document.getElementById("gift-picker-search").value || "").trim().toLowerCase();
  let filtered = players;
  if (query) {
    filtered = players.filter(p =>
      String(p.username || "").toLowerCase().includes(query) ||
      String(p.userId || "").includes(query)
    );
  }
  // Sort by play time desc (most-engaged players surface first, easier to spot
  // someone you're trying to find).
  filtered = filtered.slice().sort((a, b) => (b.playTime || 0) - (a.playTime || 0));
  if (filtered.length === 0) {
    listEl.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No match for &quot;' + escapeHtml(query) + '&quot;</div>';
    return;
  }
  const fmtMin = (s) => {
    const m = Math.floor((s || 0) / 60);
    return m < 60 ? m + "m" : Math.floor(m / 60) + "h " + (m % 60) + "m";
  };
  let html = "";
  for (const p of filtered) {
    const selected = giftPickerSelectedUserId === p.userId ? " selected" : "";
    const newBadge = p.isNew ? ' <span class="pill new">NEW</span>' : "";
    html += '<div class="gift-picker-row' + selected + '" data-user-id="' + p.userId + '" data-username="' + escapeHtml(p.username || "") + '">';
    html += '<div class="player-block">';
    html +=   '<div class="player-name">' + escapeHtml(p.username || "?") + newBadge + '</div>';
    html +=   '<div class="player-id">' + p.userId + '</div>';
    html += '</div>';
    html += '<div class="player-stats">' + fmtMin(p.playTime) + ' · 🔥' + (p.streak || 0) + '</div>';
    html += '<div class="player-server">' + escapeHtml((p.serverId || "").slice(0, 6)) + '</div>';
    html += '</div>';
  }
  listEl.innerHTML = html;
}
async function loadGiftOnlineCount() {
  // Back-compat shim: the old name is still called by target-change handlers.
  // Routes to the unified refresh so both the count and picker update together.
  return refreshGiftLive();
}
// lookupGiftUser(opts?) — opts.userId lets the picker click skip Roblox's
// flaky username resolution since it already knows the id. opts.usernameHint
// is used by the worker as a last resort if Roblox's user-info endpoint is
// also down. Without opts.userId we fall back to whatever's in the #gift-query
// input.
async function lookupGiftUser(opts) {
  const presetUserId = opts && Number.parseInt(opts.userId, 10);
  const usernameHint = opts && opts.usernameHint ? String(opts.usernameHint) : null;
  const query = document.getElementById("gift-query").value.trim();
  const card = document.getElementById("gift-user-card");
  resolvedGiftUser = null;
  refreshGiftSendState();
  if (!presetUserId && !query) {
    card.className = "gift-user-card empty";
    card.innerHTML = '<span class="gift-state-msg">Enter a username or user ID above</span>';
    return;
  }
  const token = tokenInput.value.trim();
  if (!token) {
    card.className = "gift-user-card error";
    card.innerHTML = '<span class="gift-state-msg">Set admin token first</span>';
    return;
  }
  card.className = "gift-user-card loading";
  card.innerHTML = '<span class="gift-state-msg">Looking up &quot;' + escapeHtml(query || presetUserId) + '&quot;…</span>';
  const target = targetSelect.value;
  const requestBody = presetUserId ? { userId: presetUserId } : { query };
  if (usernameHint) requestBody.usernameHint = usernameHint;
  try {
    const res = await fetch("/api/lookup-user?target=" + encodeURIComponent(target), {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", "X-Admin-Token": token },
      body: JSON.stringify(requestBody),
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    if (!res.ok) {
      card.className = "gift-user-card error";
      card.innerHTML = '<span class="gift-state-msg">' + escapeHtml(data.error || ("HTTP " + res.status)) + '</span>';
      return;
    }
    resolvedGiftUser = data;
    renderGiftUserCard(data);
    refreshGiftSendState();
  } catch (err) {
    card.className = "gift-user-card error";
    card.innerHTML = '<span class="gift-state-msg">' + escapeHtml(err.message) + '</span>';
  }
}
function renderGiftUserCard(u) {
  const card = document.getElementById("gift-user-card");
  card.className = "gift-user-card loaded";
  const statusClass = u.isOnline ? "online" : "offline";
  const statusText = u.isOnline
    ? "Online (server " + (u.serverId ? u.serverId.slice(0, 8) : "?") + ")"
    : "Offline — gift will be dropped (online-only in v1)";
  const avatar = u.headshotUrl
    ? '<img class="gift-user-avatar" src="' + escapeHtml(u.headshotUrl) + '" alt="">'
    : '<div class="gift-user-avatar"></div>';
  card.innerHTML = avatar +
    '<div class="gift-user-info">' +
      '<div class="gift-user-display">' + escapeHtml(u.displayName || u.name) + '</div>' +
      '<div class="gift-user-handle">@' + escapeHtml(u.name) + '</div>' +
      '<div class="gift-user-id">UserId: ' + u.userId + ' · target: ' + escapeHtml(u.target || targetSelect.value).toUpperCase() + '</div>' +
      '<div class="gift-user-status ' + statusClass + '"><span class="status-dot"></span><span class="status-text">' + escapeHtml(statusText) + '</span></div>' +
    '</div>';
}
async function sendGift() {
  if (!resolvedGiftUser) return;
  const setNames = getSelectedSets("gift-sets-list");
  if (setNames.length === 0) return;
  const token = tokenInput.value.trim();
  if (!token) { alert("Set admin token first"); return; }
  if (!resolvedGiftUser.isOnline) {
    if (!confirm(resolvedGiftUser.displayName + " is OFFLINE on " + (resolvedGiftUser.target || targetSelect.value).toUpperCase() + ". The gift will be dropped (online-only in v1).\\n\\nSend anyway?")) {
      return;
    }
  } else {
    if (!confirm("Send " + setNames.join(", ") + " to " + resolvedGiftUser.displayName + "?")) return;
  }
  const target = targetSelect.value;
  const btn = document.getElementById("gift-send-btn");
  const originalText = btn.textContent;
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = "Sending…";
  const label = "giveset → " + resolvedGiftUser.displayName + " (" + setNames.join(", ") + ") → " + target.toUpperCase();
  const pending = addLogEntry("dispatching " + label, "pending");
  try {
    const res = await fetch(window.location.origin, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", "X-Admin-Token": token },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        command: "giveset",
        target,
        payload: {
          userId: resolvedGiftUser.userId,
          setNames,
          initiatedBy: "AdminPanel",
        },
      }),
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    if (pending) pending.remove();
    if (res.ok && data.success) {
      // Broadcast worked, but that only means MessagingService accepted it.
      // The actual grant happens on whichever server holds the player. If they
      // were offline (or moved servers between lookup and send), no server
      // will have applied it. The hint nudges the user to verify in Studio.
      if (resolvedGiftUser.isOnline) {
        addLogEntry("✓ " + label + " — broadcast sent; check Studio Output for [BB-ADMIN] gift confirmation", "success");
      } else {
        addLogEntry("⚠ " + label + " — broadcast sent, but recipient was OFFLINE so the gift was dropped (online-only in v1)", "error");
      }
    } else {
      addLogEntry("✗ " + label + " — " + (data.error || res.status), "error");
    }
  } catch (err) {
    if (pending) pending.remove();
    addLogEntry("✗ " + label + " — " + err.message, "error");
  } finally {
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.textContent = originalText;
    refreshGiftSendState();
  }
}
async function sendGiftAll() {
  const setNames = getSelectedSets("gift-all-sets-list");
  if (setNames.length === 0) return;
  const token = tokenInput.value.trim();
  if (!token) { alert("Set admin token first"); return; }
  const target = targetSelect.value;
  if (!confirm("Send " + setNames.join(", ") + " to EVERY player currently online on " + target.toUpperCase() + "?")) return;
  const btn = document.getElementById("gift-send-all-btn");
  const originalText = btn.textContent;
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = "Sending…";
  const label = "givesetall (" + setNames.join(", ") + ") → " + target.toUpperCase();
  const pending = addLogEntry("dispatching " + label, "pending");
  try {
    const res = await fetch(window.location.origin, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", "X-Admin-Token": token },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        command: "givesetall",
        target,
        payload: { setNames, initiatedBy: "AdminPanel" },
      }),
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    if (pending) pending.remove();
    if (res.ok && data.success) {
      addLogEntry("✓ " + label + " — broadcast sent; check Studio Output for [BB-ADMIN] gift confirmations", "success");
    } else {
      addLogEntry("✗ " + label + " — " + (data.error || res.status), "error");
    }
  } catch (err) {
    if (pending) pending.remove();
    addLogEntry("✗ " + label + " — " + err.message, "error");
  } finally {
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.textContent = originalText;
    refreshGiftAllSendState();
  }
}
document.getElementById("gift-lookup-btn").addEventListener("click", lookupGiftUser);
document.getElementById("gift-query").addEventListener("keydown", (e) => {
  if (e.key === "Enter") { e.preventDefault(); lookupGiftUser(); }
});
document.getElementById("gift-send-btn").addEventListener("click", sendGift);
document.getElementById("gift-send-all-btn").addEventListener("click", sendGiftAll);
// Picker: search filters the cached list (no extra API call); refresh button
// re-fetches live data; clicking a row fills the lookup input and runs lookup.
document.getElementById("gift-picker-search").addEventListener("input", () => {
  if (giftLiveData) renderGiftPickerList(giftLiveData, null);
});
document.getElementById("gift-picker-refresh").addEventListener("click", () => {
  const btn = document.getElementById("gift-picker-refresh");
  btn.disabled = true;
  refreshGiftLive().finally(() => { btn.disabled = false; });
});
document.getElementById("gift-picker-list").addEventListener("click", (e) => {
  const row = e.target.closest(".gift-picker-row");
  if (!row) return;
  const username = row.dataset.username;
  const userId = Number.parseInt(row.dataset.userId, 10);
  if (!userId) return;
  giftPickerSelectedUserId = userId;
  // Visually mark selection in the list without re-rendering everything
  document.querySelectorAll(".gift-picker-row.selected").forEach(r => r.classList.remove("selected"));
  row.classList.add("selected");
  // Fill the lookup field for visibility, and call lookup with the userId
  // directly — the worker skips Roblox username resolution that path. The
  // list might be up to 15s stale but online status is re-verified server-side.
  document.getElementById("gift-query").value = username || String(userId);
  lookupGiftUser({ userId, usernameHint: username });
});

// Restore the last-viewed tab across refreshes. Runs last, after every const above
// is initialized, so activateTab -> startLivePolling can safely reference them.
const savedTab = localStorage.getItem(TAB_KEY);
if (savedTab && savedTab !== "commands") activateTab(savedTab);
</script>
</body>
</html>`;
